Ministry of Finance Announces Issuance of Types A and B Factory Ingots Starting Next New Year's Day 125

Central Mint Already Working Day and Night to Cast Them

Exchange of Silver Bullion for Silver Coins Exempt from Minting Fees

After our country implemented the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan, the Central Bank was ordered to announce that all domestic and foreign silver houses and money shops must report and register their stored silver bullion within one month and exchange it for silver coins. The Central Mint began casting Types A and B factory ingots, which will be issued starting next New Year's Day. Details are as follows:

Notice to Collect Silver Bullion　The Central Bank notified all banks and money shops in Shanghai that, "The Ministry of Finance has sent successive letters requesting that this bank forward a letter to the silver houses and money shops, both domestic and foreign, in Shanghai, to report the amount of silver bullion that was in circulation on the market before April 6 of this year within one month to this bank, which will then be forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for registration. After the Ministry sends personnel to verify it, it will be allowed to exchange it for silver standard coins from this bank at a rate of 715 per month." This should be complied with. In addition to having already sent a letter to the Silver Houses and Money Shops Association to forward a letter to all member silver houses and money shops to report the amount of silver bullion stored on April 6 and December 15 of this year (silver stored in other silver houses and money shops should be excluded, but silver stored in other silver houses and money shops should be included and noted), all banks and money shops that do not belong to the Silver Houses and Money Shops Association are also requested to investigate and report to this bank for forwarding. Special notice is hereby given.

Exemption from Minting Fees for Silver Coins　After the Ministry of Finance ordered the silver houses and money shops to report the silver bullion stored in the Central Bank within a time limit and exchange it for silver coins at a rate of 715, according to Article 11 of the Silver Standard Coinage Regulations, anyone who requests the Central Mint to cast silver standard coins with silver that can be used for coinage or old silver coins, such as old one-yuan silver coins that meet the original weight and silver content, will be exchanged for silver standard coins of the same value and will be exempt from minting fees. For silver with matching fineness, a minting fee of 2.25% of one yuan must be paid. If the fineness is too mixed, in addition to the minting fee, a refining fee will be added. Therefore, the exchange of silver bullion for new coins is subject to minting fees according to regulations. Now, all registered silver bullion is exempt from minting fees. This minting fee is recognized by the Ministry of Finance.

Notice to Issue Factory Ingots　The Ministry of Finance announced that, "The revised Article 12 of the Silver Standard Coinage Regulations states, 'The Central Mint may cast factory ingots, divided into Types A and B. Type A weighs 23.493448 grams, and its fineness is 999 per thousand. Type B weighs 26.6971 grams in total, with 880 parts silver and 120 parts copper, equivalent to 1,000 yuan in silver standard coins, and all are marked on their faces.' " This has been promulgated and implemented, and the Ministry has approved the forms of the two types of factory ingots and presented them to the Executive Yuan for submission to the National Government for record, and ordered the Central Mint to cast them. It is now scheduled that January 1, 1934, will be the date for the commencement of the issuance of Types A and B factory ingots to meet the needs of the market. However, Type B factory ingots are originally intended to facilitate the receipt and settlement between silver houses and money shops and are not applicable to the transfer of private individuals to show restrictions. In addition to separately informing and ordering the Silver Houses and Money Shops Association to instruct all silver houses and money shops to strictly abide by the Type B factory ingots' transfer restrictions and not to interfere with external conduct, this notice is hereby announced for all to know.

Rushing to Cast Types A and B Ingots　The Central Mint's casting of new coins is all issued by the Central Bank. Now, it has been circulated throughout the country. After the Review Committee decided to issue Type B factory ingots for the convenience of the silver houses and money shops, the Ministry of Finance approved the casting. Once the quantity is reached, it will be submitted to the Review Committee's chemist for review and handed over to the Central Bank for issuance. As for Type A factory ingots, by the end of November, 951 ingots had been inspected and qualified and sent to the Central Bank for storage, waiting for issuance on New Year's Day next year. The factory has been working day and night to rush to cast Types A and B factory ingots.

Workers at Both Wusong Factories Resumed Work Yesterday Morning 126

Central Commissioners Have Returned to Nanjing to Report Yesterday

According to the Dagong News Agency, after the entire workforce of the Wusong Zhang Huabang Road Machinery Factory and the Materials Factory went on strike on the 18th of this month, the Central Organization Committee and the Ministry of Railways sent personnel to Shanghai to mediate, and two resolutions were reached that were agreed upon by the workers. They announced a complete resumption of work yesterday morning. The Central Commissioners also returned to Nanjing by train yesterday morning to report.

Complete Resumption of Work 127

Over 1,200 workers at the Two Road Machinery Factories and the Materials Factory declared a work slowdown on the 18th of this month to protest against Mo Heng, the Chief of the General Affairs Office and concurrent Chief of the Materials Office. After the Railway Bureau and the Party Headquarters of the Two Roads submitted petitions to the central authorities requesting intervention, the Central Organization Committee dispatched Luo Meihuan, Director of the General Affairs Section, and Wang Wenbin and Zhang Weici, Counselors of the Ministry of Railways, to Shanghai to join the Railway Bureau, the Party Headquarters, and the Labor Union in persuading the workers and to reach two resolutions. With the workers' agreement, the Wusong Office and all foremen led all the workers to resume work at 7:00 AM yesterday. By 7:30 AM, the workers in each section were working as usual, and the order was quite good. The Party Headquarters and the Labor Union of the Two Roads also posted notices urging the workers to work with peace of mind. The Mo Heng issue will be investigated and handled by the Party and the Labor Union within one week and submitted to the Central Government.

Commissioners Return to Nanjing 128

After the labor unrest occurred at the Wusong Factory, the Central Organization Committee dispatched Luo Meihuan, Director of the General Affairs Section, and the Ministry of Railways dispatched Counselors Wang Wenbin and Zhang Weici to Shanghai to be responsible for persuading the workers to resume work to avoid escalation of the situation. Now that a resolution has been announced, the commissioners sent by the Central Government took the train to return to Nanjing yesterday morning to report. After the Central Government thoroughly investigates the truth, the part of the workers' accusation against Mo Heng will be handed over to the Ministry of Railways for handling.

Party Headquarters Announcement 129

The Executive Committee of the Special Party Headquarters of the Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway issued an announcement yesterday, stating that the Wu Song Machine Factory sub-office workers alleged that the director of the general affairs and material department, Mo Heng, used his position for personal gain, mismanaged affairs, undermined the labor movement, and attacked the Party Headquarters, requesting his removal from office and investigation, and advocating perseverance in waiting for a resolution. The Executive Committee expressed deep regret for the occurrence of this incident. Considering the current situation of suppressing bandits and punishing rebellion, the stability of the rear is extremely worrying. The railway is a national transportation organization, and any imprudent action can confuse public opinion. Workers have been serving in state-owned industries for a long time and have a deep love for the Party and the country and even greater enthusiasm. It is hoped that they will overcome the difficulties together and work as usual with peace of mind from now on. It should be known that supporting labor is a consistent policy of the Party. The Executive Committee should accept the workers' report of Mo Chong's undermining of the labor movement and attacking the Party Headquarters and undertake to request the Central Government to dismiss and investigate him within one week as a special announcement. All workers are hereby notified to be aware of this and not to make mistakes. This announcement.

Labor Union Announcement 130

The Board of Directors of the Labor Union of the Nanjing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Directly Under the Ministry of Railways announced that all members of the Wusong Machine Factory sub-office belonging to the Labor Union alleged that the director of the general affairs and material department of the Railway Bureau, Mo Heng, undermined the labor movement, engaged in malpractice for personal gain, and attacked the Party, and his behavior was extremely erratic, and requested the Labor Union to request his removal from office and investigation. The attitude of the members was firm and they waited for a resolution. The Labor Union was extremely saddened by the occurrence of this incident. At the time of the Fujian rebellion, the situation was extremely tense. Our two railways are the lifeline of the national industry, and any imprudent action is likely to confuse public opinion. The members have been serving on the road for a long time and have a special enthusiasm for safeguarding the labor movement. They must overcome the difficulties together and work with peace of mind from now on. The reporting of Mo Heng's various malpractices should be accepted and submitted to the higher-level Party Headquarters for submission to the Central Government, and he will be dismissed and investigated within one week. This announcement is hereby issued, and all members are notified that there should be no violations. This announcement.

Salvaging the Yuji Steamer 131

Problems with the Cargo in the First and Second Holds

The Yuji steamer of the Yu Da Company, which ran aground on Donggua Mountain in Wenzhou, has been reported in this newspaper several times. Salvage work is currently underway, but negotiations have taken place regarding the jettisoning of cargo losses. Further news is provided below.

Survey of Damage　The Yu Da Company and the Joint Insurance Office jointly dispatched the Sanjiang steamer, carrying engineers, divers, and workers, who have started inspecting the extent of the damage to the hull of the sunken ship at the scene. Divers entering the sea to investigate found two holes in the bottom of the first and second holds. Fortunately, the area is not large, and it is hoped that they can be filled. However, the hull is half-aground on the reef and half-floating on the sea surface, and there is deep concern that it may break off over time. The hull may also be in danger. Therefore, the shipowner used the thickest steel wire to temporarily secure the front of the hull to avoid accidents.

Proceeding with Salvage　According to telegrams from the shipowner and engineers, it is hoped that the Yuji can be salvaged. It may take about a week or ten days to complete the filling of the two holes in the bottom of the hold, then the accumulated water in the ship will be pumped out, so that the front hold can float to the sea surface, and it can then sail to Shanghai because the machinery between the engine rooms is not damaged at all. Currently, from the shipowner down, they are staying on Donggua Mountain to proceed with salvage work and are not taking the Sanjiang steamer back to Shanghai first.

Cargo Jettisoning Issue　The cargo loaded in the first and second holds of the ship is all olives and oranges. After running aground, they were immersed in water and completely damaged. Now, in order to repair the holes in the bottom of the ship and proceed with the pumping of water, all the water weeds in the first and second holds must be removed and jettisoned, otherwise it will be impossible to start work. Regarding the issue of jettisoning the cargo in the two holds, the shipping company notified the merchants, and the cargo owners, who had water insurance, had to notify the underwriters. This move is of great importance. The merchants have begun to negotiate with the insurance companies. The merchants' intention is that, regardless of whether the cargo is jettisoned or not, the underwriters should be liable for compensation. If the insurance companies agree, the salvage work can be carried out. As for the cargo in the rear hold, it is still intact.

Puppet State Organizes a Tourist Group 132

Invites Shanghai Business Community to Participate

What Will the Chinese People Think?

The Northeast has been seized for three years in an instant. The League of Nations' declaration of non-recognition of the puppet state has also reached all over the world. The puppet state, on the contrary, boasts of its achievements and organizes a so-called tourist group to Shanghai to entice Shanghai's domestic and foreign merchants to join the group. The Chinese people, heartbroken by the loss of their province, naturally have no intention of joining. Even foreign merchants from friendly countries, fearing the League of Nations' justice, will not want to join either. Its news is recorded as follows:

Organizing a Manchurian Inspection Group　Since the September 18th Incident, the puppet Manchu authorities have been isolated from commercial and economic relations with Guannei [Inner China] for more than three years. Now, they claim that order has been restored and that the volunteer army has been cleared, so the Japanese Travel Agency has initiated the organization of a "Manchurian" inspection group. This is the first time since the September 18th Incident. Its members are gathered in Changchun and Shenyang and come to Shanghai via Dalian Bay. The main purpose is to request Shanghai's merchants to join. The date for the inspection in Manchuria is the Chinese New Year, taking the opportunity of the rest of all sectors to ask them to visit the Northeast.

Inviting the Shanghai Business Community to Join　Half a month ago, there was news in Shanghai that the "Manchukuo" had requested the assistance of the Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai, hoping that all foreign merchants in Shanghai would send one or two representatives to join the inspection group to observe the achievements of the puppet state's governance over the past three years. Therefore, more than a week ago, the Japanese Travel Agency in Shanghai asked all merchants to send personnel to join and notified the method, and the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai also supported the agency to invite on their behalf.

Travel Expenses and Other Items Are All Waived　It is heard that "Manchukuo" will offer special treatment to the first inspection group to the Northeast, and all travel expenses for the round trip from Shanghai to Dalian by waterway, and from Dalian Bay to Shenyang by train, will be waived. The "Manchukuo" will bear all the expenses. Its purpose is mainly to have representatives of various merchants in Shanghai go to the Northeast as the starting point for the development of business and economy of "Manchukuo".

Few Shanghai Merchants Joined　Although the Shanghai merchants were the first to inspect the group after it was organized by "Manchukuo," the economy of all industries this year is in recession, and they have no intention of going to the Northeast for inspection. Even if there is no travel expense, most of them politely decline the request to join the group. Only a few representatives of certain foreign firms in Shanghai agreed to join the group, and there were very few Chinese participants.

Manchurian Group Will Come to Shanghai Soon　The Shanghai side received news yesterday that the tourist group departing from Manchuria to Shanghai has left Shenyang and is going to Dalian Bay to transfer to the sea route to Shanghai. It is estimated that it will arrive here on Sunday. The majority of the group is Japanese, and the minority is from the Northeast. The group originally planned to join a large number of Shanghai members in Shanghai to go to Manchuria together. It is heard that the stay in Shanghai is very short, and they still have to go to Dalian by sea and then transfer to the Northeast.

Regular Operation of Shanghai-Guangdong Flights 133

The company stated that despite the war,

flights will not be suspended unless absolutely necessary.

China National Aviation Corporation's routes, due to yesterday being the Yunnan Uprising Memorial Day and coinciding with Monday, had no flights arriving or departing on any routes. According to the company spokesperson, the Shanghai-Guangdong route, since the Fujian Incident, has not encountered any obstacles passing through Xiamen and Fuzhou, as the airline is purely a commercial entity. Although war has broken out recently, it has not been affected, so it continues to operate as usual. The company, for the convenience of transportation and to maintain operations, will not suspend flights unless absolutely necessary. It is expected that there will be a three-day holiday for the New Year, but flights on all routes will operate as usual during the holiday.

Lu Zhixin Sues Prostitute Yang Wenjuan 141

Yang sends letter to Lu demanding living expenses

Lu sues for attempted fraud

Yang Wenjuan, whose stage name is "Mei," was a prostitute in Minhe Lane. Because she was acquainted with local Lu Zhixin, Lu often visited her when Yang was working as a prostitute, so their friendship had a tendency to develop further. On the 14th of this month, Yang specially hired a lawyer to send a letter to Lu Zhixin, stating that Lu owed 2,030 yuan in cohabitation living expenses, and a diamond ring worn by Lu, worth 1,500 yuan. In addition, he also owed a loan of 1,000 yuan, totaling 4,530 yuan, which must be paid off within three days. He also demanded 20,000 yuan in alimony in the future. If he did not pay, he would be pursued according to law. After receiving the letter, Lu completely denied that there was any such entanglement, and immediately hired lawyer Shen Xingxia to reply in addition to the letter, and filed a criminal self-accusation against Yang Wenjuan for fraud. It was pointed out that when Yang Wenjuan was setting up a brothel in Minhe Lane, she often accompanied her friends to socialize. The defendant learned that the plaintiff had some assets and asked someone to express her willingness to commit herself as a concubine and rented a house as a place for the two to live together. The plaintiff refused because she was from a brothel and it was not appropriate to collude and tarnish her reputation. After that, he never invited guests to socialize again. The so-called "cohabitation," "living expenses," "diamond ring," "loan," etc., are not only not facts, but also have no impact. The various sections in the letter are obviously the defendant's prior fabrication of facts, hoping to intimidate out of thin air in order to achieve her intention of fraud. Her behavior is in violation of Article 363, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law, the crime of attempted fraud. Please summon the case and investigate it according to law, etc. Yesterday afternoon, judge Wu Jiazhu of the First Special District District Court opened the Fifth Court to summon the case. The defendant Yang Wenjuan was absent, and the plaintiff Lu Zhixin appeared in court with his lawyer to state the intention of the prosecution. The court then ordered the defendant to be summoned to court again for questioning at a later date.

Between, why didn't you appear in court in the Public Security Bureau? Answered, they never summoned me once from beginning to end, and this time I appeared in court, it was the court's subpoena. At this point, the official asked if you have a wife named Li Linshi, answered, yes, the official asked if there was a Li Linshi in the audience, and the woman responded and came out. The official, because she was related, ordered her to leave the seat, and then asked Li Ming, your wife Li Linshi, he said that he used to be a flower club listener, and now he doesn't do it, etc. Then his defense lawyer immediately defended that, regarding this point, Li Linshi said that there used to be a tenant who did it, and now the tenant has moved out and doesn't do it anymore, etc. The official said, this is recorded in the minutes, how can it be mixed up? At this point, the official Tieben's content of the case has not been investigated clearly, and the hall will wait for clarification before proceeding with the trial, and the lawyers on both sides rose up and requested bail, all replied that they were ill, the official said, in this case, before the investigation is clear, whether the defendants are guilty or innocent, cannot be determined, but the circumstances are very large, and the prosecution is also heavy, and bail cannot be granted, if there is a disease, the detention center has its own medical officer, or sent to the hospital for treatment, it is nothing more than serving the line only, so the court ordered not to allow it, so he ordered the defendant to sign, then Gao Maosheng said, I am illiterate, I can't write, the official said that the inspector of senior police officers is illiterate, it is really a waste of people, so he ordered to take fingerprints together, scolded the court soldiers to take them down for detention, and then continued to investigate and find out the truth, so he adjourned the court.

The situation of Chu, the district chief, sent personnel to find Li's handwriting, and after comparing it with the original presentation, the handwriting was exactly the same. Then he confirmed that the secret presentation was Yao's suspicion and instructed Li to draft and submit a presentation to the bureau for false accusation, and immediately sent police to Yao's residence yesterday, and took Yao and Li to the district at the same time. District Chief Zhang interrogated them separately. According to Yao's confession, he was 37 years old and from Shandong. He flatly denied the incident of fabricating a false accusation against Cui police officer. According to Li's confession, he was 47 years old and from Hebei, and lived at No. 40 Shenyuli. At first, he firmly denied that he had written a presentation for others to accuse Cui police officer. Later, after the district chief compared the original presentation with his handwriting, Li admitted that recently, a wharf rascal stole salted fish and was stopped by Cui police officer. The rascal held a grudge and asked someone to draft a presentation and hand it over to me to write. Afterwards, he gave me eight dimes, so the presentation was not instructed by Yao to write, etc. The district chief immediately asked Li how the rascal had someone write a presentation on his behalf, why should he entrust you to write it again, which is obviously untrue. Li was speechless at this point, so he confessed the truth, claiming that because I have been unemployed for a long time, I have been materially helped by Yao and cannot repay him. Last year, Yao planned to marry a young girl, but the girl was suddenly interfered with by Cui police officer and betrothed to Cui's nephew as his wife. Yao and Cui police officer had a feud on this matter. Yao waited until a year later, and only recently instructed me to fabricate the facts and falsely create the name Zhang Yuji, and submitted it to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to falsely accuse the police officer in order to vent his hatred, etc. District Chief Zhang obtained the confession, and Qiao mentioned Yao for questioning with Li. Yao still denied the matter. The district chief, with both human and physical evidence, immediately ordered to prepare a document to send the two defendants to the headquarters for disposal.

Two Roads Administration Improves Ticket Selling Methods at All Stations 146

Any window can purchase tickets for any station

Tickets for the day can be used on any equivalent train

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations have a total of twenty-two ticket windows at the Shanghai North Station ticket office. In the past, certain windows were designated to sell tickets for specific stations. Literate passengers do not have much difficulty, but illiterate passengers often have no way to choose among the twenty-two windows, and they often do not know which stations they want to go to are between. It is very difficult for them to ask back and forth. In order to facilitate travelers, the Administration has decided to adopt the following principles and methods: (1) All ticket windows at all stations on the two lines will not be limited to selling tickets for specific stations. That is, passengers can purchase tickets to any station at any window. (2) All windows will be open for ticket sales all day and night, so that passengers can purchase tickets for any class, any train, and any station at any time. (3) Tickets sold on the day can be used on any equivalent train on the day. (4) Stations with more windows are allowed to distinguish between the locations for issuing tickets according to the class of the ticket. However, in any case, the number of windows issuing third- and fourth-class tickets must not be less than eight-tenths of the total. (5) Ticket sellers will not distinguish between each other in principle, but for the convenience of work, they can also handle them separately according to the special circumstances of each station. The above items have been carefully planned by the Traffic and Accounting Departments, and will be implemented from January 1, 1934.

Strange News from Liuhe

Winter Wheat Bears Fruit 151

Since the beginning of winter in this city, the weather has been very warm. The temperature on the Fahrenheit thermometer is often between 40 and 50 degrees. Therefore, pedestrians on the road are all wearing camel hair or thin cotton clothes. Few people wear leather clothes. As for Zhu Jingmiao, which is more than seventy li northwest of Shanghai, in the territory of Huahe Town (in the territory of Taicang County), all the wheat planted by a certain surname and others in the northern three li of the town are on sunny highlands, and all of them are blooming and bearing fruit. It is widely spread as a strange story. According to the small wheat, it matures in the spring. It needs to bloom and bear fruit in March and April and be harvested in May. At this time, the severe winter is approaching, but it is like the spring order. It is really a strange thing, so it is specially recorded for the study of botanists.

Divorced Daughter-in-Law and Cousin Pushed Her Mother-in-Law, Causing Injury and Death 162

Lawsuit Appeal Continues Hearing Yesterday

Family Reluctant to Exhume for Autopsy

Yang Ti'an from Haimen, Jiangsu, currently 44 years old, previously worked at the Garrison Headquarters. He resided with his wife, Huang (43 years old this year), at No. 71 Hengde Lane, Dapulu, Xujiahui Road in the French Concession. His son, Yang Songpu, 24 years old this year, currently works at the Municipal Security Office. In October of last year, through a matchmaker, he married Bian Zhen from Lishui (same age as Songpu). After their marriage in Shanghai, the young couple lived with the paternal grandparents. Initially, the couple's relationship was harmonious. In the autumn of this year, a daughter was born. Bian Zhen graduated from a junior high school in the countryside and had some literacy. However, she was naturally lazy and spoiled, gradually disrespecting her paternal grandparents and husband. By mid-October of this year, the couple's relationship completely broke down. Therefore, the young couple agreed to divorce. On the 27th of that month, they invited relatives to witness the signing of a divorce agreement. The daughter born was to be raised by Yang, who would provide Bian Zhen with 200 yuan for travel expenses to return to her maternal home. After signing the agreement, Bian Zhen packed her clothes and luggage that evening, preparing to depart the next day. Unexpectedly, the next day (28th), Bian Zhen went out and met her cousin Zhao Chuan, who lived at No. 124 Taras Road in the French Concession, and her cousin Chuan Rongzhen (siblings). They told her about the divorce from Yang. Upon hearing this, the siblings Chuan and Rongzhen felt that their cousin's divorce only resulted in 200 yuan, which was too cheap for Yang Songpu. Dissatisfied, at 7 PM that evening, Chuan accompanied by Rongzhen and Bian Zhen went to Yang's house to reason with Songpu. As Songpu was out, they spoke with Songpu's mother, Huang, at the staircase entrance. A disagreement arose, and they started arguing. Chuan and the others pushed Huang, causing her to lose her balance and fall down the stairs, sustaining injuries. Chuan Zhao, Chuan Rongzhen, and Bian Zhen immediately fled. Upon learning of this, Yang Songpu and his father returned home and sought medical treatment. On the 29th, Zhao Chuan and her siblings, along with Bian Zhen, went to the police station to report that Yang had forced the divorce. The police station, considering it a civil matter, did not accept the case. Unexpectedly, Huang succumbed to her injuries and died at 10 AM on the 30th of that month. The family placed the body in a coffin and temporarily stored it at the guildhall. Yang Songpu, aggrieved by his mother's death being caused by Zhao Chuan, Chuan Rongzhen, and others pushing her, hired lawyer Zhang Qingyue to file a lawsuit for criminal injury causing death against Chuan Rongzhen and Zhao Chuan at the Second Special District Court, requesting legal action. After the court's trial, due to insufficient evidence presented by the plaintiff, the two defendants were found not guilty. Yang Songpu, dissatisfied with the original judgment, again hired lawyer Zhang to file an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Judge Sun Yunfu once summoned and investigated, stating that without examining the body, it was impossible to prove whether the death was caused by the injury and that an autopsy was necessary to determine guilt. The appellant claimed that his mother's injury had been certified by a doctor with a medical certificate as evidence, requesting exemption from the autopsy and unwilling to exhume the body again. The judge instructed the appellant to consider the matter further. Yesterday, another summons was issued, and both parties arrived on time. The judge asked the appellant Yang Songpu, "What is your decision after consideration?" Yang replied, "The people's intention is that the doctor has already provided proof, and we do not wish to exhume the body again. My grandmother also opposes another examination. However, legally, clarification is only possible after an examination. The people have no choice but to request the court to decide." Upon questioning, the appellee Zhao Chuan stated, "At 7 PM on the 28th, I sent Bian Zhen home and gave her some advice before returning home. Yang Songpu saw me out and I did not even see his mother, how could I have pushed her?" Chuan Rongzhen stated, "I have never been to Yang's house even once. Please investigate." At this point, the judge ordered both parties to leave and await further review.

Two Red Pill Operations Cracked 163

Yang Zhen from Guangdong and Ding Huqing from Changshu recently established large-scale red pill (drug) sales operations at No. 169 Lao Bazi Road and No. 24 Gongyi Fang, Beisichuan Road. Their sales were extensive. The red pills were branded as "Fortune, Prosperity, and Longevity" in red and gray colors. Their customers were mostly acquaintances or brokers specializing in this trade, selling widely in both local and out-of-town markets, yielding substantial profits. A few days ago, Chief Inspectorate Anti-Drug Department Chinese Detective Song Bingzheng discovered this and, accompanied by Western Detective Bo Pu, secretly obtained a court search warrant. They arrested Yang and Ding at their addresses. However, these two locations were merely liaison offices for customers, and no evidence could be found. Upon learning that Yang resided at No. 989 Beisichuan Road, they rushed to his home and confiscated three pounds of red pills, five pounds of gray pills, along with red pill manufacturing molds, materials, and a large quantity of morphine. They were all taken to the Hongkou Police Station early in the morning and sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin described the details, adding that defendant Ding Huqing was also involved in selling morphine for profit. In April of this year, Detective Song, who handled the case, sent an informant posing as a customer to purchase ten pounds of morphine from him. He demanded payment in advance, but the deal fell through due to the lack of such a large sum. There were several other shareholders in the operation who remain at large. An examination of the accounts revealed purchases from the Zhongwai Pharmacy of "three points" and payments to "Hongye" in September of the nineteenth year. The codes "three points" (heroin) and "Hongye" (red pills) indicated that the operation had been running for many years. He requested an extension for further investigation. The exhibits were presented to the judge, who questioned the two defendants. Their responses were evasive. Judge Wu Zehan ordered them to be remanded in custody and scheduled another hearing for further investigation.

Public Criminal Cases Not Handled by the Court

Yesterday was Christmas, celebrated by European and American countries, commonly known as the Foreign Winter Solstice. Foreign officials and merchants in the city all took a day off to hold grand Christmas celebrations. All departments of the Municipal Council also ceased operations. Therefore, yesterday morning and afternoon, all police stations under the Police Department did not send public criminal cases to the First Special District Court for trial. Although the court was scheduled to operate as usual on the anniversary of the Yunnan Uprising, due to the current national crisis, it was ordered to remain open. In the morning, the court only handled private criminal cases, which was relatively less busy than usual.

Yonghua Store Burglarized After Closure, Goods Worth 20,000 to 30,000 Gold Stolen 166

Discovery Made After Half a Year of Closure

Thieves Possess Extraordinary Abilities, Police Intensifying Investigation

The Yonghua Department Store at No. 428 Xinqiao Street, Fadama Road, managed by Tan Huisheng, went bankrupt this summer due to financial difficulties. Creditors filed a lawsuit with the Second Special District Court, and the store was sealed. After half a year, the creditors reached an agreement with the store owner and requested the court to lift the seal so business could resume. The store owner first sent people to clean and tidy the store. However, upon inspection, goods worth 20,000 to 30,000 gold had been stolen. Shocked, they reported to the police, who dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. They found a large hole in the roof. They also found a large hole dug in the wall of the adjacent Yuantong Shoe Store at No. 91 Xinqiao Street, covered by a wooden cabinet. According to the shoe store owner, the front of the building was rented to a person surnamed Fang in September, who left behind old furniture and belongings last month without saying goodbye. Later, they received a postcard stating that the furniture was used to offset the rent. They then sublet the space to a person surnamed Zhang and were unaware of the theft. The detectives reported the situation to their superiors, who ordered them to apprehend the thieves for investigation. It was reported that when Yonghua Company sent people to clean the store, they also found a pot of freshly cooked rice in the kitchen stove, which had been eaten, and a quilt on the sofa. This indicates that the thieves had been occupying the store day and night, boldly selecting and stealing goods at will. Such a large-scale theft is unprecedented, and it is impossible for only one or two people to have committed it. The police are now conducting a thorough investigation to apprehend the thieves and bring them to justice.

Woman's Earrings Robbed, Police Fired a Shot Before Apprehending the Thief 167

Gao Jincheng, a local, lived on Dapulu in the French Concession. Yesterday morning around 11 AM, Gao, along with his mother and wife, went to the China Hotel on Guizhou Road and rented a room to bathe. Around 1 PM, they left the hotel together. Gao had a bicycle, which he could use for transportation. He hired rickshaws for his mother and wife, while he followed behind. When the rickshaws reached Fuzhi Lane near Shantou Road, Guangxi Road, a robber suddenly emerged from the lane and forcibly tore off Gao's wife's gold earrings and fled into the lane. Gao's wife cried out in pain, shouting "Catch the robber!" Gao rode his bicycle and chased after the robber into the lane on Shantou Road. At that time, the robber was escaping from the same location. Upon seeing Gao, he turned back and ran away. Gao noticed a police officer nearby and reported the incident. The officer drew his gun and chased after the robber. As they approached Guangdong Road, the officer was very close to the robber. The officer ordered him to stop, but the robber continued to run. Fearing that he would escape, the officer fired a shot at the robber, hitting him in the leg and bringing him down. The original stolen goods were recovered, and the robber was taken to the police station. Due to the severity of his injuries, he was transferred to the hospital and will be dealt with after he recovers.

Thieves Demand Compensation for Reputation 169

Qian Tanglao Caught Stealing Official Clothes

Chen Erlang, a resident of Meimen, who resided at No. 3 Jumei Lane, Bailinan Road in western Shanghai, earned his living working in a biscuit factory. On the morning of the 22nd of this month around 9 AM, while he was out shopping, he saw a man who often visited the Chen family, who were tenants on the same floor, carrying a large bag of clothes, hurriedly leaving the house. At the time, Chen Erlang did not think much of it, assuming he was a friend of the tenants. Unexpectedly, at 12 PM, Chen and his wife returned home for lunch and found that their clothes had been stolen. His wife cried out about the theft and inquired among the other residents. The tenants on the upper floor, surnamed Chen, had also had their silk and leather clothes stolen, totaling more than twenty pieces. Chen Erlang then told them what he had seen and learned that the man was named Qian Tanglao. They went together to Qian's place to investigate, but Qian denied everything. Chen Erlang went to various pawnshops nearby and found that two of the stolen clothes had been pawned at the Qiantai Pawnshop on Robert Road. Under Chen Erlang's name, they had pawned goods worth 15 yuan, and under the name of the tenant Chen, goods worth 25 yuan. They also confirmed that the clothes and appearance of the person were indeed Qian Tanglao. The tenant Chen felt that Qian was a fellow villager and friend, and his reputation was at stake. After Chen Erlang persuaded him, they immediately prepared the pawn money and redeemed all the clothes to put an end to the matter. Unexpectedly, the thief Qian Tanglao did not have the good fortune to enjoy his freedom. Instigated by his accomplice Liu Genliang, he went to the tenant Chen a few days ago to negotiate, forcing him to compensate the landlord Chen Erlang for damages to his reputation in an attempt to extort money. Chen Erlang felt that since he had witnessed him carrying the bag out and the pawnshop had confirmed it, he still dared to come back and extort money. When he loudly rebuked him, it happened to be when Team Leader Tang Bingxiang and Detective Zhou Wenhai from the Sixth District Detective Team were patrolling nearby. After inquiring about the situation, they apprehended the two thieves, Qian Tanglao and Liu Genliang, and took them back to the district. They also searched Qian's home and found the original stolen cash, 38 yuan (only 2 yuan had been spent), all with the pawnshop stamp. After questioning them separately, the district officer considered that the thief had stolen in broad daylight and then tried to extort money, which was truly despicable. He immediately prepared a document to send to the bureau for trial.

Second Branch Warden Jiang Fengyi Transferred 172

Jiang Fengyi, the warden of the Jiangsu Second Branch Prison behind the First Special District Court in this city, has been ordered by the Ministry of Justice and Administration to be transferred to the post of Warden of the Zhenjiang County Prison. The vacancy will be filled by Qiu, the section chief of the Nanjing Jiangsu First Prison, who will come to Shanghai to take over the position. The original Zhenjiang Warden will be transferred to fill the vacancy of Section Chief Qiu in the Jiangsu First Prison. Since Mr. Jiang took office as the warden of the Second Branch Prison in Shanghai in July of this year, he has actively improved the internal operations. When he took over, it was during the hot summer, and the prisoners were extremely crowded. After Mr. Jiang's planning, a temporary detention center was set up on Tiantong Road to alleviate the congestion. He strived for cleanliness in the prisoners' diet, hygiene, and medical care. As a result, although there were hundreds of prisoners, there were few reports of illness. The Second Branch Prison's work aspect for prisoners has never been well-developed. Since Mr. Jiang took office, he has urged progress, and it has seen a rapid increase, exceeding more than double. He also had clear rewards and punishments, not showing favoritism. He is truly a talented person in the prison industry, and Chinese and foreign people have praised him. This winter, fearing that the prisoners' clothing and bedding would be insufficient, he has donated more than one hundred sets of cotton clothes and dozens of cotton quilts from various philanthropists so that the prisoners will not suffer from the cold. Warden Jiang's dedication to prison administration and his guidance of prisoners to repent and reform are truly worthy of public service. It is regrettable to hear that the transfer is imminent. Good officials do not last long. It is also heard that Mr. Qiu has been ordered and will soon come to Shanghai to take over the position.

Educational News From Other Regions

Ministry of Education Explains Regulations for Secondary School Graduation Examinations 180

Regulations for Examination Committee

—Instructions to the Jiangsu Education Department—

The Jiangsu Education Department submitted a request to the Ministry of Education for clarification on ambiguities in the regulations for secondary school graduation examinations and the rules for the examination committee. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education instructed the department, stating, "We have received your submission. We will now address the questions you raised point by point as follows: (1) If secondary schools under the jurisdiction of education departments or bureaus in various provinces and cities have classes that begin in the spring, graduation examinations must be held twice each year. Students who repeat a grade may participate in the subsequent examination. Therefore, repeating a grade twice is equivalent to repeating one academic year. If parents are unable to bear the cost or students do not wish to repeat the grade again, the original school may issue a certificate of completion. (2) Senior high schools are permitted to admit students with equivalent academic qualifications, as explicitly stipulated by the Ministry in the secondary school regulations. There is no need to reiterate this in the examination regulations. Junior high school students who fail one or two subjects may use their equivalent academic qualifications to take examinations for higher education. (3) Graduation examination passing certificates are not graduation diplomas. The school’s certificate will be produced by the department and issued within two weeks after the examination for students who pass to use for applying to higher education. As for graduation diplomas, they should be marked with the words 'Examination Passed'. After verification and stamping by the department, they will still be issued by the original school. (4) Members of the examination paper setting committee and the proctoring committee must not be appointed from the faculty and staff of schools participating in the examination. Please comply accordingly."

Ministry of Finance Remits Funds for Primary and Secondary School Education in Beiping City 181

(Nanjing, 25th) Primary and secondary schools in Beiping City repeatedly telegraphed the Ministry of Education to double the central government's subsidies. On the 25th, the Ministry of Education replied to the representatives of primary and secondary schools in Beiping City, approving the Ministry of Finance's response that 25,000 yuan in subsidies for November for primary and secondary schools in the city had been remitted to Beiping.

Tsinghua Graduate School Experiences Dispute over Sending Students Abroad 182

Jiang Tingfu Does Not Recommend Qualified Students for Overseas Study

Zhu Yanfeng States Reasons to the University President's Council

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) The first graduating class of Tsinghua University's graduate school, having been reviewed by the faculty and deemed qualified to graduate, has been recommended to the President's Council in accordance with Article 14 of the graduate school's charter for approval to be sent abroad. These include Lu Xueshan, Shao Xunzhen, and Shao Xunge. Zhu Yanfeng, a graduate of the current class of the graduate school, is involved. For this selection of students to be sent abroad, the Ministry of Education ordered that five students be sent. However, only four students meet the requirements of Article 14 of the graduate school's charter, including Zhu Yanfeng. According to the charter, he should also be sent abroad. He has twice appealed to the President's Council and University President Mei Yiqi. The President's Council has now replied that because the director of studies, Jiang Tingfu, did not approve him, his request is still not approved. The entire faculty and student body is tense about this. Our reporter made a special trip to Tsinghua University to investigate, and the situation from all sides is described as follows:

Inside Story of Sending Students Abroad This year's selection of graduate students to be sent abroad by Tsinghua University is based on Article 14 of the graduate school's charter, which states, "Graduate students with a three-year grade point average of 1.05 or higher, and with graduation examination and thesis scores of 'Superior' or higher, may be recommended to the President's Council by the department head." This year, there are six graduate students, but only four meet these three criteria. The Ministry of Education ordered the university to send five students. Beforehand, the general opinion within the university was that the number of students sent abroad would be either five or four, and certainly not three. The history graduate school has two graduates, Zhu Yanfeng and Shao Xunzhen, whose grades both meet the standards for recommendation. According to the charter, they should both be recommended to the President's Council by the department head. However, the department head, Jiang Tingfu, did not recommend Zhu Yanfeng. When Zhu questioned Jiang, Jiang said that the charter states "may be recommended," which also means "may not be recommended," so he has the right to decide. In order to uphold the law and protect students' rights, Zhu had no choice but to appeal to the President's Council for an interpretation of the charter. The President's Council replied, "Regarding the recommendation of graduate students with 'Superior' or higher grades to the President's Council, the Council discussed it last week and generally agreed that the procedure should be subject to the department head's review. Not all students with 'Superior' or higher grades must be recommended to the President's Council." Therefore, there is still no resolution.

Zhu Yanfeng's Petition For the matter of application, I have learned that graduate students to be sent abroad have already been recommended by each department to the President's Council. However, I was not nominated by the history department head, which surprises me greatly. I have checked my grades, and they are sufficient to meet the recommendation criteria, but I have not been recommended. I do not know the reason for this. I have sent a letter to Director Jiang Tingfu, requesting a remedy. According to Director Jiang's statement, this is a matter of interpreting the law. Since the graduate school charter states "may be recommended" by the department head, that means the department head may also "not recommend." Therefore, the director has the power to decide. However, if the president or the President's Council believes that there is another interpretation and a supplementary recommendation is required, then it can be handled accordingly. According to the opinion of most students, the phrase "may be recommended by the department head" should be interpreted as follows: the opposite of "may be recommended" is "may not be recommended," not "not recommended." "Not recommended" is the opposite of "recommended." "May be recommended" is said in continuation of the preceding text, meaning that only if the grades meet the "may be recommended" standard can the director "may be recommended." Otherwise, the director "may not be recommended." Therefore, "may be recommended" and "may not be recommended" depend on the student's grades, and not on the arbitrary decisions of one or two individuals. In other words, it should be based on objective judgment and pursue what is right. Therefore, although the word "may" cannot be said to be equal to "should" on the surface, it actually contains the spirit of "should." If the grades reach the legal standard of "may be recommended," then the director has no legal reason to believe that he "may not" recommend them. I sincerely hope that the president and the council will uphold justice and correct the history department head's misunderstanding, so that I may receive a supplementary recommendation. I am most eagerly awaiting a response. Respectfully submitted to the President's Council and President Mei. Student Zhu Yanfeng respectfully submitted.

Ministry of Education Issues Circular that Midwifery Schools Graduate in Three Years 184

Those with excellent facilities and complete curriculum

—May be approved to graduate in two years—

(Nanjing, 25th) The Ministry of Education issued a circular to all provinces and cities on the 25th, stating, "The Midwifery Education Committee previously submitted a request to order subordinate senior midwifery schools to set the length of study to two years. However, the Vocational School Law and Regulations promulgated by the Ministry stipulate that all senior vocational schools graduate in three years. Midwifery schools are of great importance to the health of mothers and infants. Most schools do not have perfect facilities and curricula. Therefore, three-year graduation should still be the standard. If senior midwifery schools in each province and city have excellent facilities and complete curricula, they may be approved to graduate in two years after approval by the Ministry. Please forward this to your subordinates for compliance."

Ministry of Education Investigates Students Studying Abroad in Various Countries 185

(Nanjing, 25th) The Ministry of Education sent a letter to all Chinese embassies abroad, stating, "There is a lack of complete records and statistics on Chinese students studying in various countries over the years, making it difficult to obtain information. It is also inconvenient for judicial, administrative, and examination agencies to inquire about the qualifications of students studying abroad. It is now planned to start by investigating Chinese students studying in various countries in the past ten years. A special form has been prepared and attached to this letter. Please translate it and send it to schools above the specialized level in various countries where you are stationed, asking them to fill it out, or ask the highest education administrative agency in the country where you are stationed to conduct the investigation."

Ministry of Education's Committee on People's Education Solicits Opinions on Plans from Various Committee Members 186

(Nanjing, 25th) The Ministry of Education's Committee on People's Education will hold a meeting at the Ministry of Education starting on January 11th. The people's education plan and various regulations have been sent to committee members Chen Lifu and 17 others, asking them to sign and provide their opinions.

Ministry of Education Sends Letters to Middle Schools Across the Country to Investigate Science Experiment Equipment 187

(Nanjing, 25th) The Ministry of Education believes that the science equipment in secondary schools in China is rudimentary and that a minimum standard should be set. The Middle School Science Teaching Material Discussion Conference co-sponsored by Jinling University and Ginling Women's Arts and Sciences College is requested to set equipment standards for mathematics, physics, and biology in senior and junior high schools. The survey form for student experiment teaching materials for physics, chemistry, senior high school biology, and junior high school zoology and botany, drafted by the conference, has been sent to middle schools across the country, hoping to be filled out and sent to the Ministry of Education within one week.

Zhejiang Provincial Library Prepares Cultural Relics Exhibition 188

Celebrating the 30th Anniversary of the Library's Founding

Exhibition of Fine Books, Rubbings, Pictures, and Other Cultural Relics

—December 30th to January 3rd—

In recent years, the Zhejiang Provincial Library has been quite effective in improving facilities and increasing readership. At the same time, it has also been committed to preserving documents and promoting scholarship. Now that the library has reached its 30th anniversary, in order to commemorate the past and encourage the future, it has been decided to hold a 30th anniversary celebration on December 30th. In order to expand viewing and promote scholarship, a cultural relics exhibition will be held for four days from the next day to January 3rd of the new year. The preparatory situation is described as follows:

The founding of the Zhejiang Provincial Library can be said to be at the forefront of the trend in various provinces. The allocation of the Siku Quanshu (Complete Library in Four Sections) of the Wenlan Pavilion 150 years ago (Qianlong 47th year) allowed scholars to view and copy, which opened the precedent for modern libraries. Later, during the Taiping Rebellion, the pavilion was destroyed and the books were damaged. The old rules were restored only after Ding's collection and repair and Tan Fu's construction. However, this was still a special system, and the transmission was not widespread. It was not until the 29th year of Guangxu (1903) that Zhang Hengjia, the Zhejiang academic administrator, at the request of the gentry of the county, founded the Zhejiang Library, hiring Yang Fu as supervisor, widely collecting new and old books, and formulating reading and borrowing regulations, which is the power of today's provincial library. It has been 30 years since then. In order to commemorate the past and encourage the future, the library has decided to hold a 30th anniversary celebration on December 30th, and a cultural relics exhibition for four days from December 31st to January 3rd. The content of the exhibition will focus on fine books, supplemented by rubbings, pictures, ancient artifacts, calligraphy, etc., and special attention will be paid to items related to the sages of this province. Sources of exhibits In addition to various books and rubbings from the library's collection, rare items are also being collected from collectors in the provincial capital. Among them, the fine book section includes the Song edition of Famous Ministers' Tomb Inscriptions Wan Yan Collection recently purchased by the library, old Song, Yuan, and Ming editions, various manuscript copies of Siku Quanshu, Yongle Encyclopedia, and essential books from all sides. The rubbing section includes rubbings related to the anecdotes of this province and other rubbings, Han and Wei stone carvings rubbed by the Shandong Library, rubbings newly purchased from Beiping, and rubbings of calligraphy printed by the Chunbei Ge Tie Stone recently collected. The picture section includes various paintings, cultural relic photos, and exquisite illustrations from British and German documents. The National Art College also has art books in its collection participating in the display. Artifacts and calligraphy are displayed as attachments, and many volumes and albums of inscriptions and inscriptions related to the sages of this province have been collected. In order to highlight the achievements of predecessors and show the progress of the past 30 years, a special library history exhibition is set up to display various old archives and souvenirs. Although the library is unable to expand the scope due to the unstable situation and the heavy workload, it only started preparing one month ago. However, in order to broaden the knowledge of all sectors of society, it deeply feels that the rare books in the collection are too few, so it plans to collect items from collectors in the provincial capital. Yang Fu, Yu Shao, Song Sunjun, Gu Bainian, Wang Xiu, Fan Zhen, and others have responded, and the items from the Wang family in Changxing are the most numerous. According to the exhibition, exhibitions are often held in Pingjin. Exhibitions on cultural relics are rare in the south. The Zhejiang Provincial Library held a Ding Songsheng cultural relics exhibition last autumn to commemorate Ding Songsheng. Now, taking advantage of the library's anniversary, there is this cultural relics exhibition, which is enough to set the tone for Hangzhou. The time coincides with the New Year, and not only will various agencies and schools in the provincial capital be on holiday and easy to visit, but also people from Shanghai can take a short trip to the lake during the holidays and have the opportunity to visit at the same time.

Local News

University Education Association Initiates the Organization of a Thrift and National Salvation Association 189

And Issues a Declaration on Thrift and National Salvation

The Shanghai University Education Staff Union, including Chu Minyi, Zhang Shouyong, Weng Zhilong, Zheng Hongnian, Yan Fuqing, Li Denghui, Hu Puan, Kang Xuanyi, Lin Zhongke, Lei Guoneng, Zhang Jixin, Qiu Hanping, Jiang Zhensan, Chen Jilie, Long Tiyao, and more than 40 others, initiated the organization of a Thrift and National Salvation Association, which was unanimously passed by the tenth joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees. The declaration is recorded below:

Declaration of the Thrift and National Salvation Association Since the September 18th Incident, the Northeast has fallen, and Pingjin is in danger. The people of the country are heartbroken, and the national crisis is urgent. Everyone is thinking of ways to save the country. However, the efforts to resist aggression have been repeatedly launched and defeated. The reason for this is that there has been no sufficient preparation in peacetime (once an emergency occurs, we rush to meet the enemy with flesh and blood, facing sharp weapons. The success or failure is known without the need for wise people). The enemy is advancing step by step, getting an inch and wanting a mile. Everyone understands that they will not be satisfied with what they have already obtained today. America's three-year naval construction plan and Russia's construction of fortresses and deployment of troops along the border are all based on the fact that our country has lost thousands of miles of territory within two years, and the violent invasion has no end. They are also indirectly threatened and cannot but actively prepare for national defense and consolidate their surroundings. Recently, an agreement has been reached between the United States and Russia to join hands to prepare for the earth-shattering storms in the Pacific Ocean in the near future. The United States and Russia are known for their strength in the world. Once they feel an indirect threat, they rush to catch up, fearing that they will not be able to do so. However, looking back at our country, which is weak and directly impacted, what is the state of its national defense?

Preparing for National Defense is Primarily About Economy The ultimate source of the economy lies in the people. Therefore, enriching the national economy is the primary task of saving the country today. As for the methods, they are nothing more than two aspects: increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. However, the way to increase revenue is extremely difficult, and long-term plans cannot be done in a moment. However, reducing expenditure is easy, and all of our people, if they are determined, can implement it and achieve results at any time and anywhere. The undersigned is not talented, but wants to start with the negative reduction of expenditure to gradually move towards the positive increase of revenue. This is the origin of the Thrift and National Salvation Association. The simple method is to save our unnecessary expenses to enrich the general national economy, so that the majority of the people do not feel the pressure of life, so that everyone has spare strength to engage in the path of saving the country. However, the way to reduce expenditure is extremely complicated and difficult to list one by one. What the undersigned is paying attention to is

The Most Superficial and Simplest Things It is not to say that these few things have exhausted the way of thrift. After all, strict thrift is not something that everyone can bear. Now, we first choose a few things that everyone can abide by, and use them as broad creeds to promote them. If they are effectively implemented, the results will be considerable. As for those who can be more frugal and thrifty outside of this creed, they are the ones that the undersigned prays for most earnestly. Furthermore, the way of thrift should not only be actively carried out after the current national crisis, but also should be advocated in order to eliminate the root causes of future national crises. In today's society, extravagance is the norm, and competition is for vanity. The salaries of public officials often do not cover their expenses. As a result, bribery and corruption are heard of every day, and the spirit of integrity is completely swept away. How can we purify the officialdom if this is the case? Furthermore, in the case of ordinary citizens, due to the temptation and constraints of the extravagant environment of society, life is becoming increasingly difficult. Those who commit crimes are increasing day by day, and society is becoming increasingly decadent, with no hope of revival. Because of the corruption of politics and the decay of society,

Its Impact Extends to the Countryside For thousands of years, the countryside, which we have relied on as the source of life, is now in danger of bankruptcy. As a result, from large cities to remote villages, no one is not suffering from the pressure of life. Finance is exhausted, and purchasing power is decreasing day by day. The existing industries and businesses are struggling to survive, and the development of new businesses is out of the question. If this continues, even without foreign aggression, it will be difficult to maintain ourselves. How can we avoid the side-eye of our strong neighbors? Based on this, our task of thrift is not only to cope with the current national crisis, but also to correct future bad habits to establish a stable national foundation. Its organization should be long-lasting, and its scope should be broad. We hope that our fellow countrymen will not hesitate to give instructions and actively participate, so that everyone can easily lift the weight, and the country and society will be fortunate. The association's constitution is omitted for brevity.

In addition to holding a national goods parade on New Year's Day next year, a Women's Friendship Conference will also be held, with the sole aim of promoting national goods, hoping that female compatriots will all have the determination to use domestic goods, which will be beneficial to the national economy and the people's livelihood. This is a special notice."

The County Education Association Urgently Seeks to Develop Rural Education 194

Submitting Proposals to This Year's Education Administration Committee

Promoting Women's Education and Designating Leader Schools

Zhang Yi, representative of the Shanghai County Education Association, has submitted many important proposals to this year's Education Administration Committee in order to develop the county's education. The original proposals are recorded as follows:

Promoting Women's Education Proposal for Promoting Rural Women's Education (Reasons) According to a recent survey, the number of literate people in rural areas accounts for 16.3%, and the number of illiterate people accounts for 83.7%, especially women. Therefore, rural women's education is extremely important. Looking at the people's schools that have been established in our county, the number of female students is always less than the number of male students. Without special facilities, it is difficult to promote it. A proposed method is used to request a public decision. (Methods) Train teachers for rural women's education, set up special women's schools, and focus the curriculum on daily use, such as textile sewing, knitting, medicine, literacy, and bookkeeping. Borrow village houses as classrooms, equip them with application tools, and ask for special assistance if the teachers are not capable enough.

Determining the Education Center Proposal for Determining the Education Center for the 23rd Year (Reasons) If the national education bureau does not have a definite center, then the thoughts of its citizens will inevitably be scattered. Regarding the current situation of the national society and our county, it is very urgent to develop people's livelihood and enrich national power. It is up for public decision whether to determine the education center for the 23rd year as the place for production education. (Methods) The county education bureau should invite experts to formulate an implementation plan, submit it to the province for record, and carry it out effectively.

Designating Leader Schools Proposal for Designating the Third, Fourth, Fifth, and Sixth Districts as Leader Schools (Reasons) The central system in the first and second districts of this county has already been implemented. Due to the relationship between education funds and the environment in the third, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts, no central schools have been established. In order to seek joint education and promotion in one district, it is necessary to designate leader schools. (Methods) The county education bureau should select a school from the existing schools in the third, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts as the leader school and formulate methods to jointly promote the work when things happen.

Yesterday, Jiangda Football, Jiaotong, and Fudan Won 198

Jiaotong Defeats Jinling 4-1

Fudan Defeats Central 3-0

—Only Remaining Match in the Entire Schedule: Jinan vs. Fudan—

The Jiangda football tournament, with the Central and Jinling universities coming to Shanghai to compete, has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, the two teams played against Jiaotong and Fudan respectively, and both visiting teams suffered crushing defeats. As a result, Jiaotong defeated Jinling 4-1, and Fudan defeated Central 3-0.

Jiaotong Defeats Jinling. The match was held at Jiaotong University at 2:30 PM. Jiaotong's entire line was well-organized and extremely aggressive. Although Jinling also had strong players, under Jiaotong's attack, Jinling was seen to be faltering. After a quarter of an hour, Jiaotong's Zhou Guangzhong scored the first goal. Afterwards, Jiaotong's offense became even more fierce, constantly harassing Jinling's territory. Zhou Guangzhong scored the second goal, and Wen Liandong scored the third. The first half ended there. In the second half, Jinling tried to rally, but the situation was still unbalanced. Although Jiaotong had several more opportunities, they all missed. Jinling resisted strongly, launching several counterattacks. Finally, with only one minute remaining, Lin Jianxue scored a goal for Jinling, avoiding a complete rout. The lineups were as follows:

Fudan Defeats Central. The match between Fudan and Central was held at the municipal stadium in the city center. The field was flat and wide, with thick grass, comparable to a baseball field. The match was quite intense, with both sides having opportunities, but neither scored. Fudan's strength was originally quite formidable, but they were unable to win for a time. The first half ended without any goals. After the break, Fudan rallied and was determined to win, while Central suddenly found itself struggling to defend. The enemy's presence was dense in front of their goal. Fudan raided and pillaged, with extremely rampant momentum. Finally, Yu Shunzhang scored two goals in a row. Although Central tried to counterattack repeatedly, their forward line felt weak, and they were limited by Guan Laoye's impregnable defense, with no opportunity to take advantage of. In a renewed effort, Fudan's An Lesheng also scored a goal, defeating Central 3-0.

Shenyuan Charity Football Match: China Defeats West United 4-2 201

China Scores Three Consecutive Goals in the Second Half to Reverse the Defeat

West United Suffers Defeat Due to Lack of Cooperation Among Star Players

Auction of Football Raises a Huge Sum of 500 Yuan

In yesterday's inaugural match of the Shenyuan Football Field, a Sino-Western charity football match, the Chinese team defeated West United 4-2. Over ten thousand spectators cheered and danced with joy. The Chinese team defeated the West United All-Star team, and although the Chinese team was trailing 1-2 at the end of the first half, they were able to rally in the second half and score three consecutive goals, reversing the defeat and winning the McKinley Silver Cup. Mayor Wu personally attended the opening ceremony and performed the ceremonial kickoff. After the match, Mayor Wu auctioned off the football to raise money for charity. Mr. Gu Liren of Yuyuan Road generously donated a huge sum of 500 yuan to purchase it, setting a new record for charity football match auctions. His righteous and courageous actions are commendable.

Intense Battle with Few Highlights. Both sides were the elite of Chinese and Western football, and their performances were naturally top-notch. However, due to injuries and other commitments, Wan Xianghua was unable to play for the Chinese team due to the Jiangda competition, so the Chinese lineup was not at its best. West United was assembled on short notice, and cooperation was difficult, so there were not many highlights. However, the battle was intense throughout and was still interesting. The Chinese team was behind in the first half and was under constant attack, so it was already in a dangerous situation. After scoring in the second minute of the second half, they made it 3-2, and the dangerous situation turned into jubilation. West United launched a fierce counterattack but eventually ran out of steam, and the situation went from intense to tiring. In the last five minutes, Li Yichen's goal brought excitement to the otherwise dull situation, creating a perfect ending.

Chinese Team Captain Sun Jinshun Holds the Silver Cup (Photo by Qichang) 202

West United's Defeat Was Unexpected. Due to the incomplete Chinese lineup and the fact that West United was made up of elite players, the pre-match predictions were worrying for China. Some even said that the result would be a huge 4-0 or 6-2 score. However, the opposite happened. West United's defeat can be analyzed as follows: too many defensive errors, weak right midfield, and a complete lack of cooperation among the forwards. Xu De and Tao Lehui did not pay attention to the flanks and made too many mistakes. For example, the fifth goal was Xu De's mistake. Stoke was not good at playing as a winger in midfield, and his contribution yesterday was too little. Among the forwards, the wingers were slow and unable to cooperate with the two famous players Maolin and Aqiao from Vasas. As a result, cooperation broke down. Walter could not run, and Willie's passes all went out of bounds. In terms of individual performance, Smith stood out, and goalkeeper Herbert made many saves.

Chinese Players Deliver Satisfactory Performance. Looking back at the Chinese team, it was not easy to achieve this result. Careful play and full effort were the main reasons for the victory. The performance was also unexpected. Goalkeeper Xu Heng is improving day by day. The two defenders had some minor flaws, but they were not a problem. Midfielder Xu Yahui is still a star, and Chen Zhenxiang was able to cope and worked very hard. Among the forwards, right winger Chen Jiaqiu was the most outstanding, dominating his side. Although Sun Jinshun has iron legs, his shots were not on target. Dai Li's shots were just as good. Gu Shangkuang, who switched from defense to wing, cannot be said to have been derelict in his duties, but he was a little slow.

West United Opens the Scoring with Bluster. After Mayor Wu performed the ceremonial kickoff, the Chinese team kicked off. The ball was passed far to Jiaqiu. West United countered, and Aqiao shot. It was saved, and Gu Shangkuang advanced fiercely on the left. Tao Lehui made two mistakes, but both were unsuccessful. The Chinese team still had many chances to attack. Once, Jiaqiu passed the ball to Linjing, who was about to shoot but did not succeed. Yichen intercepted the ball and shot at the goal, but it flew wide. Dai got a pass from Jiaqiu and shot at the goal again, but Herbert caught it and slipped, still not scoring. West United countered, and Keleite shot from the right. Xu Heng caught it and bounced it out, and Aqiao slammed it into the net. It was already half an hour.

Pulling Back a Goal and Then Conceding Again. After losing a goal, the Chinese attack was fierce, surrounding the enemy's goal and applying great pressure. Jiaqiu got help from Yahui, and Yichen came to attack the goal. Xu De turned around and sent it out, but the ball did not go far. Sun Jinshun shot again, but Stoke, who was useless, actually had an effect at this time. The ball happened to bounce off Stoke's body and then bounced off the goalpost. Otherwise, it would have gone in. In the melee, Chen Zhenxiang sent a long kick, which cleared the danger again. Five minutes later, after Sun Jinshun was offside, Li Zaichen passed to Gu Shangkuang, who passed it back to the center. The Chinese center then scored with one shot. Just as one wave subsided, another rose. Walter advanced on the left, and the ball went to the right area. Li and Jiang, the two defenders, were momentarily stunned, and Keleite attacked unprepared and gently deflected the ball. Xu Heng thought it was out of bounds, but it happened to go into the goal. The first half ended there.

China Rallies and Scores Repeatedly. In the second half, Aqiao and Smith immediately started a fierce attack. The defense cleared the danger, and the Chinese players were seen to be active again. Gu Shangkuang got the ball and went straight in. Xu De came to block, dodged past, passed to the center to Dai, and then Li Yichen took it into no man's land and rushed into the goal. Within these two minutes, the score was tied. The Chinese team rallied from this, and their morale soared. Both wings were very active, and West United was in a very difficult situation. Five minutes later, Li Yichen got a pass from Sun Jinshun and scored again, making it 3-2 and taking the lead. Cheers erupted.

At the End of His Rope, Dai Scores Again. West United then paid attention to defense. Smith monitored the Chinese center Dai, never leaving his side. Leimi also retreated and did not come out, switching from attack to defense. The forwards became increasingly isolated and useless. At the end of his rope, they were completely desperate. In the last five minutes, Jiaqiu attacked the goal. Li rushed up to head the ball and collided with the goalkeeper. The ball was punched out, and Xiao Dai followed up with a shot, making it 4-2.

Auction of Football Raises 500 Yuan. After the match, Mayor Wu and Mr. Geli Mu Xu, chairman of the Westerners' Association, gave speeches, encouraging the players in the field and thanking the guests outside the field. After the speeches, Mayor Wu presented the huge McKinley Cup to Chinese team captain Sun Jinshun. After the cheers of ten thousand people, Wu held up the football and stood on a chair, auctioning it off in a loud voice. Just as the value was being discussed, land merchant Gu Liren stepped forward to purchase it. His bid was 500 yuan, and no one in the entire field contested it. It was settled, exceeding the ball price of last year's charity competition by 300 yuan. It can be seen that the level of concern for charitable causes among the people of Shanghai is indeed advancing day by day.
