San Francisco Sino-Japanese Rugby Match 210

Chinese Team Loses 12-13

Old Grievances Unresolved, Overseas Chinese Do Not Support the Competition

Organizer Heavily Criticized and Will Leave to Avoid the Situation

(Havas, San Francisco, 24th) In the rugby match held here between the Chinese and Japanese teams, the Japanese team won 13-12. Historically, there has been a match between the Chinese and Japanese teams every year, but it was suspended after a brawl in 1930. Today, very few overseas Chinese attended the match. Chinese team leader Mr. Lin announced that the Chinese team's defeat made him feel ashamed and that he planned to leave San Francisco immediately. He also said that only 18 of the Chinese team's thirty-odd members agreed to participate, and the overseas Chinese in the city refused to provide assistance. One of the Chinese team members, Mr. Long, a former University of California player, claimed that the game was originally a draw. Although the Japanese team was dominant after the start, the Japanese were leading 13-6 two minutes before the end of the game. At this time, the Chinese team counterattacked and scored a try, thus regaining six points, making it 12-13. According to the rules, each team can kick the ball after scoring a try. If this kick is successful, one more point can be scored, resulting in a tie. Unexpectedly, the Chinese team's final kick, although it fell on the goal line, the referee did not make such a judgment, causing the Chinese team to lose by one point.

Spring and Autumn

Bump 211

— Only Via

The red-headed Asan dodges three zhang high, wielding the red and green traffic lights at the crossroads. Thus, trams don't bump into cars, horse-drawn carriages don't bump into field cars, and rickshaws don't bump into bicycles. Although the road is like a tiger's mouth, country folk carrying hobnailed shoes and umbrellas can still walk safely and avoid the danger of "bump".

"Bump" is the most dangerous thing in the world, because the results of a bump are always unspeakable and unmentionable.

The soft bumping into the hard is like a mantis trying to stop a chariot, overestimating its ability. Therefore, smart people don't take immediate losses. From afar, seeing a fast-moving car, they stand on the sidewalk and wait for the car to pass before crossing the road. Seeing someone raising a stick to hit people, they still run away as early as possible. Those who play with pens have to give way to those who play with guns, because pens are made of bamboo, and guns are made of iron, with a big difference in hardness. These are all "compasses for avoiding magnetic fields".

In fact, the "compass for avoiding bumps" doesn't need to be promoted, it's already well-known to everyone. And even if the soft inevitably bumps into the hard, or doesn't have time to avoid it, and has to bump, at most, the soft will have a bloody head and broken bones. It doesn't affect the public. So what is extremely worrying for social security and the future is nail heads bumping into iron heads, hard bumping into hard.

Bombs are hard, and soil is soft. If a bomb falls into the soil, the soil shows a big hole, and everything is fine. But if a hard bomb falls on a hard cement building, without politeness, the bomb explodes, the building collapses, and people and livestock are destroyed together. This is the terror of hard bumping into hard.

Patrols catching hawkers, hard sticks bumping into soft flesh. If the soft flesh avoids the hard stick, there will never be trouble. Patrols catching robbers, everyone has hard guns and bullets, and no one is willing to avoid that hard bump. Under this bump, both sides are hurt, which is naturally expected, and it is not impossible for innocent pedestrians to be sacrificed under this bump. Therefore, we hope that bandits disappear, so that when we walk on the tiger's mouth-like road, we have to avoid "bumping" into cars and horses, and also be careful of hard stray bullets bumping into us.

Dream 212

— Chuan Zhaoyang

Dreams are great and unbelievable. In dreams, we can be the winner of a 500,000-dollar lottery; I can kill the enemies we hate in dreams. If we feel that life is too bland, dreams can give us a tortuous and strange world. If we feel dissatisfied, dreams can give us 120,000 points of satisfaction. Dreams are sacred!

Because dreams have such benefits, no one doesn't want to dream. Everyone tries their best to dream. They can sacrifice wealth, people's respect, their own morality, and even their own lives to seek the satisfaction of dreams.

However, we all know that dreams will not continue to infinity. There will always be a time when dreams wake up. The satisfaction gained in dreams will become a movie after waking up, disappearing in an instant. But people always pursue dreams like that.

China is a world of dreams. No one in China is not living in a dream. They want to become rich; they want to be important people; they want to immerse themselves in happiness. They forget the sadness when they wake up from their dreams, they only care about some tiny pleasures in their dreams.

Bombs cannot wake up the Chinese people's dreams; artillery shells cannot wake up the Chinese people's dreams. It seems that as long as there are dreams, the Chinese will be so satisfied, and nothing else matters.

However! Dreams always wake up! Let go of those poor pleasures in dreams! Let's not wake up only after the enemy's guns are aimed at our chests!

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 214

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 20: Fortune-telling Brings Smiles to the Old Man's Face for Days; Endless Worry Remains with the Old Friend Across the Street

Guizhi finally realized what was happening and said with a smile, "I noticed your face was sallow and thin like this, and you're always sick, so I got anxious in my heart. It's really just making a fuss, does getting anxious make the illness go away?" Madam Jiang smiled and said, "Oh! You understand that yourself, then I don't need to say more." Guizhi suddenly thought to herself, "I should cheer myself up." So she scooped a basin of hot water and washed her face clean. Besides applying a layer of snow cream on her face, she also took out two long-unused rouge blocks from the drawer and applied two red blushes to her cheeks. She combed her hair neatly, curving the short hair that covered her face behind her ears and securing it with small hair clips. When she looked in the mirror again, her face was radiant, with no sign of illness. To make herself look presentable, she simply took off her blue cloth jacket and changed into a clean one. Madam Jiang, seeing this from the side, thought she was going out, so she said, "That's right, it's good for you to take a walk around the block, so you don't get sick from being cooped up." Guizhi smiled and said, "I'm not going anywhere. I'm afraid people will see me and think I'm not sick, so I just washed my face." Madam Jiang said, "It's good for you to go out for a while. People who sleep too much should get some fresh air." Guizhi also felt flustered and bored, and since her mother had said so, her feet took her to the front door without her own control. But as soon as she reached the front door, the Gan family's gate was directly in front of her, and she was immediately startled. Originally, she was going to walk on the road towards the Gan family's gate, but then she turned her face away and walked in the other direction. After walking a few steps, she unconsciously sighed and shook her head, saying, "It's really a curse. Why can't I let him go in my heart?" She walked forward step by step, looking at the road under her feet. She could almost distinguish every clump of grass and every stone. Occasionally, she looked up and saw a young man in a worn Western suit, wearing a wide-brimmed felt hat slightly askew. He held a thin bamboo cane in his hand, swinging it from side to side in front of him, walking with uneven steps, also looking very bored. Guizhi suddenly stopped and exclaimed, "Huh?" The man also suddenly looked up, and they met each other's gaze. It turned out to be Gan Jizhi himself. She wanted to avoid him, but she ran into him. Darn! Isn't this a case of enemies meeting on a narrow road? (277)

The Tumbler 215

— Qian Xuecun

"Tumbler, the old man does not fall; nod him, he rises; push him, he does not fall."

These few lines are what I read in elementary school; but now, thinking back, they have a very profound meaning.

Speaking of the tumbler itself, it is a wax shell toy made for people to play with. However, you should not therefore despise it; it has a kind and pleasant face, no matter how people bully it, it will never be angry, always smiling. It is completely a philanthropist, and it can also be said to be a great statesman. In particular, when people nod it, then it nods, but rises immediately after nodding; when people push it, it leans to the side, but it does not fall. In this way, it is also a hero; it can bend and stretch, and has an indomitable spirit of fearlessness, just like the martyrs and generals of ancient and modern times, both domestic and foreign.

As for China, it has hundreds of millions of square miles of area, which is thousands of times better than the tumbler's wax shell. And China always treats people with a kind and pleasant face. No matter how other countries bully it, it is always kind and still smiling at people. From this point of view, China is a great charitable country; but it cannot be called a great political country. However, when people nod it, then it sleeps for a long time; when people push it, it falls and cannot get up. In this way, China is a coward, how can it have the ability to bend and stretch like a tumbler, and the indomitable spirit of fearlessness?

Alas! Can it be that China is not as good as a tumbler?

Copper Coins and Silver 216

— Yiyi Guan Zhu

"Copper coins and silver," who doesn't like them? Although, some people keep saying, "Copper coins and silver should not be taken too seriously," which is true. But, strangely enough, the more people who say "copper coins and silver should not be taken too seriously," the more their eyes will widen and bulge out when they see "copper coins and silver." What is the reason for this? Some people say: this sentence "copper coins and silver should not be taken too seriously" is originally "words of sarcasm" spoken to others! If they say this to themselves as well, and really take "copper coins and silver" lightly, then I am afraid it would be a little difficult to find such a fool in this materialistic world, even with a lantern and a broken foot warmer lid!

Originally, what do all living beings do? To put it bluntly, it is still for "copper coins and silver!" "Poor people" who have no "copper coins and silver" certainly cannot relax their grip on "copper coins and silver," and even dream of them. Look, all year round, all day long, on the roads, those who cannot take cars, or those who are walking, come and go, who is not busy for "copper coins and silver!"

As for "rich people" who are rich in "copper coins and silver," they should, in principle, be able to stop chasing after profit. However, it is not so, they still have to be busy, and even busier! On one hand, the abacus beads are rattling away, all day and all night. On the other hand, their minds are filled with the idea that "the more copper coins and silver, the better." Naturally, people like this take "copper coins and silver" so seriously that if you ask them to take some out to do charitable and public welfare work, forget it! Because they swear that they would never think that once they leave this world, no matter how precious "copper coins and silver" are, they will never go with them! That is to say: they are left to their children and grandchildren, and the result is that they only provide their children and grandchildren with the means to choose evil and do wrong! Then what is the point?

Alas! But, in this chaotic world, how many people can see through this point?

Short Story

Wane and Wax (Part 1) 217

— Tian Hensheng

Fifteen years ago, Li A'quan's five-year-old daughter, Xiaoling, was betrothed to Yu Mingfa's seven-year-old son, Longsheng, through the matchmaker Jiang Si'die. After the Jiang and Yu families agreed to the engagement, Mingfa invited Zhu Changchun, who ran a millet shop next door, to be the assistant matchmaker because matchmakers had to come in pairs.

At that time, Li A'quan was very poor and relied on an old boat that was about to fall apart as a tool for making a living. The family of three lived on that old boat, and everything was simple and crude. In terms of food, even the bowl for serving rice had a chipped edge, and they couldn't afford a new one. In terms of lodging, they didn't even have a mattress, only a quilt that was patched with countless patches inside and out, and the cotton batting had many holes, making it stiff and offering little warmth. The three of them covered themselves with the quilt during the nights on the vast water, and before winter even arrived, the cold wind mixed with the chill of the water directly entered the cabin, already causing them to shiver. Before A'quan's parents died, there were three rented rooms on land, and there was more than one boat. A'quan's father didn't often personally sail out. He only needed to rent out a few boats to others, collect some rent, and that was enough for the family's expenses, with plenty to spare. Unexpectedly, his parents died one after the other, and a fire burned down the three ancestral rooms. He had to sell the boats; when he sold until he was left with only the last old boat, he had to rely on it to make a living, so he endured not selling it, preferring to suffer the harassment of the lien holders and his own lack of food and clothing. So A'quan started his career on the water, loading and unloading goods for others, sometimes east, sometimes west, without a fixed route. Since his daughter Xiaoling was engaged to the Yu family, he wanted her to be raised in their home as a child bride. He thought that his daughter would eventually belong to someone else's family, and since he was so poor now, why should he let her suffer? Moreover, his boat was used to load and unload goods for others, and having a child was inconvenient. His motivation for asking Jiang Si'die to be the matchmaker was to have her raised in the Yu family's home after the engagement, to spare his daughter from suffering and to ease his parents' worries, as living on the water was not as safe as living on land, and children were prone to danger. However, after the engagement was made, when he asked Jiang Si'die to express his wish to the Yu family, the Yu family refused to raise her as a child bride. At the same time, Xiaoling's mother suddenly couldn't bear to let her only darling leave her, and she was a little resentful of the Yu family's refusal to raise her as a child bride. After some time had passed, someone rented his boat to transport hundreds of bags of flour, and the matter was dropped.

A year and a half later, A'quan's boat finally returned to his hometown. He went ashore to see his new in-laws, Yu Mingfa, and was kept by his new in-laws for a drink and a meal. They talked about what had happened since their last meeting, and it wasn't bad. Although A'quan was illiterate, he was a very straightforward person. He told Mingfa that he had prepared the ten silver dollars he borrowed from Wang Changxing, as well as other small debts, and was ready to repay them. He didn't necessarily have to return home this time, but he did so to pay off these debts, and to meet his in-laws and see his new son-in-law. Indeed, he was very fond of this son-in-law and specially brought a few toys from afar, and gave him a silver coin when they met. As a result, the mother-in-law was also happy. The next day, he also went to meet the two matchmakers, Jiang Si'die and Zhu Changchun; he took money to repay his debts everywhere; he didn't even have time to visit a few relatives, and on the third day, he sailed away again. This time, it was more than two years before he returned, and his circumstances were about the same as they were two years ago.

Free Talk

A Brief Discussion of Heroes 218

— Fengzi

Since the beginning of history, China has had heroes in every generation. And they are certainly able to reshape the times, so the ancients said: "Heroes create the times."

This is probably true. When the world is in great chaos, there must be evil-doers, and the great achievement of destroying the evil-doers must be attributed to the heroes. Therefore, after Li Zicheng and Zhang Xianzhong, there had to be a Qing Emperor who quelled the bandits, conquered the Ming dynasty, and pacified the Central Plains, so the people "brought baskets of rice and jars of drink to welcome the royal army."

What is being welcomed with "baskets of rice and jars of drink" is usually the royal army, and the royal army is still the same group of killers. The one who commands this royal army, needless to say, is the hero.

The hero leads the royal army, mightily marching into the pass, not only killing for a while, but also sowing seeds, ready to kill for generations to come. The Han people truly deserve to be "bearing the burden of humiliation" subjects, they don't mind a few deaths. Moreover, killing is the hero's natural duty, and the dead are still fated to suffer.

Those who are fated to suffer are certainly supposed to die, and those who are endowed with killing skills are said to have some background. Therefore, heroes mostly belong to celestial stars. Stars like Ziwei, Wuqu, and Baihu, as long as their mortal hearts stir, they will be sent down to the lower realm to be heroes for a time. Therefore, ordinary people are just ordinary people, and the conditions for being a hero must be innate.

Once the term of exile is over, the celestial stars return to their positions. Then another batch comes down.

However, the Chinese people mostly do not admire contemporary great men, but like the heroes of previous dynasties. Luo Tong's great battle with his intestines hanging out, Wu Song single-handedly capturing Fang La, and even the Black Whirlwind, wielding two axes, killing his way into Jiangzhou City, hacking at everyone he met, regardless of officers, soldiers, or civilians. Speaking of it, it always feels somewhat satisfying, as if there were no bloody scenes at all. But Luo Tong and Wu Song lost their lives because of this: the Black Whirlwind killed for a while, but still had to escape to Liangshanbo. Only the Qing Emperor killed with such grandeur, and not only was he not harmed, but he actually benefited. It can be seen that it is possible to be a hero, but the method must be carefully considered. The one who paid the most attention to the method of being a hero was Cao Mengde. He specially ran to an astrologer to ask for advice. The astrologer knew that he was a great hero, but added that he was "a capable minister in times of peace, and a great hero in times of chaos." Mengde also knew that it was a chaotic time at the time. His heart couldn't help but be very happy. Jin Shengtan probably missed a point, because this was probably "setting the stage" for the later discussion of heroes while boiling wine.

In addition, there was Huan Wen, who said "If I cannot leave a good name for a hundred generations, I will leave a bad name for ten thousand years."

But what I am talking about is the Qing Emperor.

On Criticism 219

— Shiheng

Recently, there have been quite a few articles discussing criticism in magazines or newspaper supplements. But summarizing the opinions in these articles, they are generally nothing more than this: it is hoped that critics will not speak out of personal emotions, but should only discuss the work itself, and even more so should not use criticism as a weapon for personal attacks. The opinion expressed implicitly in such articles is that, although there is great dissatisfaction with the current critical articles, there is also a very strong hope for criticism, for fair criticism that can satisfy people. This can be said to represent the opinion of the majority of people - no one does not hope for this.

The fact that writers or readers feel very disgusted with the current criticism and cannot help but complain about it is the responsibility of the current critics. However, in today's Chinese literary world, the objective conditions for the emergence of better critical articles are insufficient. I think that those who write critical articles should also bring this up for general complainers to refer to.

First, it is most unfavorable to criticism to generally regard personal attacks and scolding as criticism, and then criticize criticism, because this view is likely to make people develop an incorrect view that there is originally a category of scolding in criticism, and the scolders themselves also think that they are doing criticism. As a result, the more scolding there is, the less criticism there will be. Secondly, shouldn't we reflect on whether we have been indirectly encouraging scolding in the past critical world while welcoming it? - Looking at the past critical debates, we cannot help but say that the more tasteless and scolding they are, the more people like to participate in them, come to watch the battle, and the more meaningful ones, everyone keeps silent. And even some people, although they are constantly scolding on the one hand, are also criticizing criticism and criticizing scolding criticism on the other hand! The scolders and the critics of criticism have formed a unified body, and the result is that we only see the destroyers of criticism and cannot find the builders of criticism.

Furthermore, although true criticism is currently in the minority, it cannot be said to be absolutely non-existent: why don't we take these as topics for discussion, and instead only talk about those criticisms that we do not think are criticism? Ignoring true criticism and only taking scolding criticism as a topic, makes true critics feel lonely and makes scolders more active, which is tantamount to rewarding scolding.

The Street Performer 220

— Zhou Lengjia

Having found an empty abandoned square, the street performer put down the magic tricks he was carrying on his shoulder, put down the old-fashioned weapons in his hand, and also put down the child he had depended on for several years.

He had been wandering in the world since he was young, until his forehead was covered with wrinkles from life. He watched his wife die, his daughter run away with someone, and he himself fell from the position of selling medicinal plasters by demonstrating boxing skills to making a living by performing magic tricks and wielding weapons. Every time he thought of this unhappy life, the street performer's heart would ache faintly.

"Chang! Chang!" The street performer struck his only one-handed gong, and the sound of the gong carried the wail of his life. The rhythm was tragic and desolate.

More and more people gathered to watch the fun, and finally formed a large circle.

Standing in the center of the circle, the street performer routinely clasped his fists, speaking the formal greetings of the trade. He had said those words countless times, and they were almost memorized by heart. Every time he re-chewed those words, his heart would be saddened. How difficult it was to get rid of the burdens of life!

Performing martial arts alone in front of the audience, the street performer's heart was lonely. At the same time, the rust on the weapons aroused his sadness even more: this seemed to symbolize his real life. The glorious era of shining was over, and what reality had left him was only this rust. He thrust the weapon into the ground, and a desperate cry almost burst out of his mouth.

After performing all his skills, the reward he received was only some contemptuous "boos." No one threw down a single copper coin. In such a situation, the street performer had no choice but to swallow his anger, dragging the weapon back to the place where he had put down his props. The thought that "old and faded things are worthless" quickly flashed through his mind, causing him to completely lose the courage to open his mouth and beg for money.

After this initial failure, he then had the child take the stage. The child was only eight or nine years old, very short, but used all his strength to swing his fists and feet, and clenched his teeth to do somersaults, tiger jumps, and standing on his hands. Watching the underage child risking his life to perform tricks for the sake of survival, tears began to well up in the street performer's eyes.

However, the desires of the onlookers were satisfied. They treated other people's pain as a kind of pleasure. If this child could bleed to death in front of them due to overexertion, then they would definitely throw copper coins like crazy. Just because he wasn't quite at that point yet, although the cheers were loud, only a few scattered copper coins were thrown down.

In order to get a few more coins, and also in order to satisfy the audience's cruel psychology, the street performer began to order the child to strip off his upper body in the cold wind, lie on a large vat used for magic tricks, and he himself held a rusted green dragon knife, using the back of the knife to hit the child's back heavily. The back of the knife was thick and cold, and every time it hit, the child would let out a painful groan, and the skin on his back would turn from white to red to purplish. Immediately, the audience all screamed "good!" and copper coins rained down on the ground. However, the street performer seemed not to see it. He only felt that the back of the knife in his hand was not hitting the child, but his own heart. Every time it hit, his heart felt as if it had been cut with a knife, and it was so painful that it was unbearable.

As it got dark, the audience gradually dispersed, and the street performer ended the scene with his familiar set of formal greetings. He contentedly collected the copper coins on the ground, reloaded the props on his shoulder, held the weapon in his hand, and the other empty hand stretched out involuntarily, caressing the child's injured back as he was putting on his clothes.

"You've worked hard! Child, let's go!"

After saying these few short sentences, the tears that had been hidden in the street performer's eyes for a long time finally couldn't help but roll down his cheeks.

Book Talk 221

— Junzhi

(1)

During the Jiajing reign, there was a Jinshi named Zhu Dashao, who loved to collect books, especially Song dynasty woodblock editions. Once, he visited an old family in Wumen, which had a Song edition of Yuan Hong's "Later Han Records," which was a hand-annotated copy by Lu Fangweng, Liu Xuxi, and Xie Dieshan. He very much wanted to obtain it. Unfortunately, the other party would not sell it, leaving him helpless. Finally, they managed to reach an agreement: he would exchange it for a beautiful maid. This maid could write poetry. Before leaving, she wrote a poem on the wall:

Without reason, I am given up from my deep chamber,

It is still better than when people in the past exchanged horses;

If we meet again in the future, do not be sad,

The spring breeze will blow away the roadside branches.

Dashao, after reading this, felt regret, but for the sake of the Song edition book, he had to "give her up." This matter is seen in "Xun Zhi Tang Za Chao," and Lei Gong once quoted it in his work "Nen Wo Bi Ji."

(2)

Zhu Yizun (Zhuzhai) was also a book lover. He once did a very interesting "stealing copy" thing. That was because Qian Muzhai had many secret manuscripts copied by hand, which he took with him wherever he went and did not easily show to others. Zhuzhai had repeatedly tried to get them but failed. One night, Muzhai went to a banquet outside, so Zhuzhai took advantage of this opportunity to bribe Muzhai's "page," "opened the lock and placed dozens of copyists in a secret room in advance, and they copied it in half a night, and then returned it." Of course, this matter was later exposed. The matter of Zhuzhai's "stealing copy" was therefore spread all over the north and south of the Yangtze River.

Two Brothers (70) 222

— By Maupassant, translated by Li Weike

"No, my child, that's impossible. It would condemn both of us to hell. I've tasted that punishment for the past month. You're moved now, but when that emotion passes, when you look at me the way 　er looks at me, when you remember what I've told you... Ah... my little Zhean, just imagine... just imagine I'm your mother!..."

"I don't want you to leave me, Mother, you're all I have."

"But, my child, you must think about how we'll never be able to look at each other again without blushing, I'll feel ashamed to death, and your eyes will make mine droop."

"That's not true, Mother."

"Yes, yes, it is true! Ah! I understand all the inner turmoil of your poor brother, all the inner turmoil from the very first day. Now, when I hear him come into the house, my heart leaps as if it will burst through my chest, and when I hear his voice, I feel like I'm going to faint. Back then, I still had you! Now I don't have you either. Ah! My little Zhean, do you think I could live with both of you?"

"Ah! Ah! How is that possible!"

"Yes, it is possible."

"How can you expect me not to think of this when I see the two of you? Will you not think of it yourselves, you two?"

"Me, I can swear!"

"But you will think of it every moment of every day."

"No, I swear to you. Besides, listen to me: if you leave, I will kill myself." She was simply terrified by his childish threat, she embraced him, caressing him with passionate tenderness. He went on to say:

"I love you more than you can imagine, much more. Come on, don't be silly. Just try staying for eight days and see. Will you promise to stay for eight days? Surely you can't refuse me that request?"

She placed her hands on Zhean's shoulders, straightened her arms, and grasped his arms, saying:

"My child... let us be calm, not emotional. Let me speak first. If I ever hear you say the things I've heard from your brother's mouth this past month, if I ever see in your eyes the meaning I've seen in his eyes, if I ever sense from a word or a glance that I am as hateful in your eyes as I am in his... an hour later, do you hear, an hour later... I will leave and never return."

"Mother, I swear to you..."

"Let me speak... for a month now I have been suffering the pain that one person can endure. From the moment I understood that your brother, my other son, was doubting me, and that he was guessing the truth minute by minute, every moment of my life has become a torment I cannot explain to you."

Her voice was so heavy with sorrow that Zhean was infected by her pain, his eyes filled with tears.

He wanted to embrace and kiss her, but she pushed him away, saying:

Securities Lack Chips, Bond Market Squeezed Higher 224

Consistent Increase of 4-5 Jiao to 1 Yuan, 3 Jiao, 5 Fen

Yesterday at the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange, because the futures for this month only had two days left, those on both the long and short sides with insubstantial positions, although not numerous, experienced a more intense short squeeze than before. During the squeeze, chips did not diminish in their tendency to be squeezed due to their small quantity. This was because in recent days, many of the long positions rolling over had been fully 　 prepared. The short side had demand, but there was little supply, leading to a sense of depletion of chips. The shortage of gold futures in July, when a shortage of 20,000 to 30,000 units raised the off-exchange price to 72 yuan, served as a grim reminder. Therefore, the short side's covering became increasingly difficult the later it was done. This is a situation often seen during a short squeeze. Yesterday, in terms of news, there was not much progress or retreat in the war situation. Since the central government ordered Qiao Min of Fuzhou to withdraw, the war gradually entered the main force battle, entering the third act period since the warlord uprising. Yesterday morning at the opening, most of the activity was helping the short side to cover, and long positions rolling over were rare. Chips suddenly appeared scarce, and market prices increased consistently by several jiao to one yuan. Before the second session, various items in the front row continued to rise by 3-4 jiao due to demand. The back rows fell slightly by 3-5 jiao due to some short selling. There were also many temporary sellers. In the afternoon, because Zhang Ji and others arrived in Shanghai and reported satisfactory results, people's hearts remained firm. Only grain fell slightly by 3-4 jiao, while the rest continued to rise by 2-3-4 jiao. At the close, various groups had sporadic needs, and the short side covered later, market prices increased again consistently by 3-5 jiao, and the upward trend was likely to continue. As a result, market prices increased consistently by 4-5 jiao to 1 yuan, 3 jiao, 5 fen. Trading volume totaled 19,282,000 yuan, including 2,000 yuan in spot goods, futures excise salt tax totaled 6,720,000, 　　accounting for 3,390,000, 19th period totaled 2,370,000, 20　20 open totaled 3,250,000, gold short 　6　 accounting for 2,100,000, and the rest ranged from several tens of thousands to 300,000 to 400,000. Today is the last day for December futures.

Silk and Tea 246

Silk Cocoon Merchants on the Verge of Bankruptcy

Statistics show that silk cocoon mortgages have reached about 10 million yuan

Foreign firms' silk sales are in a slump. Silk mills in Jiangsu and Zhejiang have accumulated large stocks of silk that cannot be sold. Due to the need for expenses, they have temporarily mortgaged their remaining cocoons and silk to banks and pawnshops. Statistics show that this has reached about 10 million yuan.

North China Tea Sales Are Picking Up 247

Our country's tea, in addition to being manufactured and sold by foreign firms, is also shipped to Beiping, Tianjin, Yingkou, Qingdao, and other ports, amounting to more than 200,000 dan. Since recently, the sales of foreign firms have almost completely stagnated. However, stores and firms in North China have recently been sending telegrams requesting to purchase various types of green tea, such as Songluo maoqing.

Shipping Export Report 255

▲Qingbo Class

Tong Taixiang Hongyi and other tea firms have transported a total of more than 4,200 bags to Tianjin, Shandong, and other ports in recent days, which is a significant improvement compared to the previous months.

A Large Quantity of Japanese Tea Imported into Kulun 256

Kulun is a commercial center in Mongolia. The tea trade there is controlled by Russians. In recent years, Russian merchants in Shanghai and other ports have handled Zanxi green tea and floral brick tea, which are sold to Mongolia, amounting to no less than 100,000 dan. However, this year, more than 60,000 dan of Japanese green tea have been transported to Mongolia by Russians. The reason is that green tea is expensive, while Japanese tea is cheap and can be completely purchased on credit. In the future, various types of green tea, such as Zhuang Gongxi Yuanzhu, will be greatly affected.

Actively Investigating and Prohibiting Fake Tea in Wenzhou 257

Eradicating the bad habit of adulteration and fraud on one hand

Improving production and sales methods on the other hand

In recent years, our country's tea exports have gradually decreased, and prices have also been declining. Tea farmers have found it unprofitable, and the bad habit of adulteration and fraud has become increasingly prevalent. Farmers in the Pingyang area of Wenzhou annually export fake tea, which, according to investigations, amounts to about 2,000 dan. Although most of this fake tea is sold domestically, it has a significant impact on the reputation of tea in an invisible way. In view of this, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, in addition to prohibiting the export of several batches of tea that were found to be fake this year, also notified the Zhejiang Construction Department to strictly prohibit local officials. On the one hand, it also notified Chinese and foreign tea merchants in this city to pay close attention. At the beginning of this month, it also took advantage of the opportunity of Mr. Lu Yunfu, who was sent by the Rural Reconstruction Committee of the Executive Yuan, to investigate the tea industry in that area, and entrusted him to conduct a thorough investigation. After Mr. Lu arrived in Wenzhou, he immediately went to Beigang, the central area of fake tea production, with Magistrate Zhang of Pingyang County to carry out publicity. The local people have all expressed regret. At the same time, he ordered the tea merchants in the area to organize a tea industry association, which must automatically prohibit fake tea production from next year, otherwise, they will be severely punished. According to Mr. Lu's investigation report, there are many types of fake leaves adulterated in that area, among which the leaves of cold danxin, liujing, hongchaixin, camellia oleifera, and loushanning trees are the most common. The method of prohibition is to passively prohibit it on the one hand, and on the other hand, to continue to find ways to improve production and sales, so that tea farmers can have profits to make, then fake leaves can be eliminated invisibly.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Talking About Tolerance 258

— Mo Tu

Tolerance is something the Chinese have always admired.

Although there is no teaching in history to turn the other cheek after being slapped on the left, proverbs like "let it dry on your face after being spat on" have long been spread as admirable stories. This kind of tolerance is unique to the Chinese.

But it's not the same in foreign countries. There are few people who can be so generous, let alone have such great magnanimity, and it can be quite petty. Just look at the recent ban by the Dutch East Indies government on the import of firecrackers from our country to know. The reason for restricting imports is said to be because most of them contain powerful gunpowder, which is very dangerous (the original text can be found in the report on March 21).

Everyone knows that firecrackers are just a kind of toy. Although "most of them contain powerful gunpowder", the amount is limited. At best, they are only used to scare imaginary ghosts. I have never heard of firecrackers replacing artillery shells and grenades. Its colorful appearance and loud, impressive sound are not even feared by children. Moreover, most of those who set them off are Chinese, which has nothing to do with the economy of the Dutch East Indies. However, the Dutch East Indies government is so careful, thinking that it is "very dangerous" and restricting its import. If this is not because the foreign masters do not know the goods, then it is a matter of tolerance.

Looking back at our country, millions of "powerful gunpowder" guns are imported from overseas every year, but our general public, although living under artillery fire every day, seems to be used to it and does not feel "dangerous" at all about this huge annual import of murderous weapons, nor have they ever prohibited it. On the contrary, there are those who have offered their blood and sweat to provide capital for this trade for the general public. Hasn't the money and grain in Sichuan Province been pre-levied for more than sixty years of the Republic of China, and suffered four hundred seventy-eight or nine (according to Shanghai Weekly, the author has removed one digit, and there is a new record since the author stopped writing.) civil wars? Paying money to buy guns that "mostly contain powerful gunpowder" to fight wars, and even sacrificing one's own body as a target, isn't this tolerance big enough?

But there are also those with little tolerance. That is, those who play with guns and cannons often "cannot stand beggars asking for food". If they are not polite, they must compete. This is naturally said to be within the country. To the outside world, they will still return to the tolerance of "give them whatever they want". We are originally a nation that loves "peace"!

The Misunderstanding of Mr. Li 259

— Rain

It's only been within the last month that my friend Mr. Li has entered a passionate love life. Because an supreme authority has suddenly been established in his mind, his life is clearly more organized and richer than before. The usually messy front room has now become well-arranged; a vase with fresh flowers has been added to the tea table, sparse and well-placed pictures hang on the wall, and in the glass frame on the desk, his own shadow has been replaced by a smiling angel holding a flower. Even the pillowcases have been replaced with new ones, exquisitely embroidered with "My Dear" and initials as a shortened signature.

The complete makeover of the room unmistakably hints to anyone with a little bit of awareness that the owner of this house is undoubtedly "in love"!

One Saturday evening, Mr. Li kissed his beloved goodbye, full of joy, and returned to his apartment. The clock showed it was almost nine. He lit a cigarette, and as he leisurely smoked, he dreamily recalled the warmth and sweetness he had received from her throughout the afternoon.

The "tap-tap" of high heels grew louder and closer in the alley below, finally knocking on the door of his own apartment. The evening visitor did not arouse any attention in him. Because his beloved would definitely not come at this hour, and he had no other female friends who would visit at this time. He then heard the knocker talking to the maid downstairs, looking for "Mr. Li." However, this was not strange at all; there really was another "Mr. Li" on the second floor, but that "Li" was currently in the hospital getting his nose operated on.

But, tonight's visitor was beyond his expectations. The "tap-tap" of leather shoes went straight up to the third floor! With one further step, there was a gentle knock at his door. "Misty Li!"

"How strange!"—as he mentally drew question marks and exclamation points, he opened the door to greet the "unexpected guest."

"Whom are you looking for?" he asked as he greeted, sizing up the female visitor from head to toe. She wore a magenta serge skirt, with a flannel shirt, commonly worn by overseas Chinese students, tucked into the waistband. The round neckline revealed a smooth, fair neck. Her face was round, and although not very beautiful, the contrast of her clear, watery black and white eyes brought her "overall average" score to no less than seventy points.

"Is Misty Li at home?"

"He lives on the second floor, went to the hospital the day before yesterday. Is there anything I can..."

"Oh! He's in the hospital? Yes, he's always been weak and sickly..."

This friend surnamed "Li" knew that the female guest had made a "double booking" mistake, because he clearly knew that the Misty "Li" in the hospital was a "big guy" who was not "weak" at all. But he couldn't explain it directly, so he could only vaguely say a few words to send her on her way.

"He probably won't be back for a day or two. You can leave a note, or go to the hospital to find him tomorrow. The hospital is at..."

"Alas! I have something very urgent. I live in the Jiande Academic Society and owe six dollars in rent—we're all away from home, don't let your husband laugh at me—" (as she spoke, she forced a shy expression), "Today the servant refused to open the door for me! That Mr. Li used to promise to help me, but now he's sick, leaving me with a problem for tonight..."

"You can go to find him tomorrow..."

"But, tonight... Can you help me a little, sir?..."

"I'm very sorry! I only have fifteen coppers left!"

"Then... my accommodation problem tonight can't be solved! Could I borrow a room here for one night? I'm in trouble! Besides, you and I are both from high society, so male-female relationships are not a problem..." As she spoke, her facial expression gradually turned from "solemn" to flushed.

"This... originally it wouldn't be a problem, but, I am a married man. My wife teaches in Suzhou and always comes to Shanghai on Saturday evenings, so there's no way. I'm sorry..." he lied as he pointed to the photograph.

The strange female visitor pestered him from nine o'clock until half-past ten, leaving disappointed and empty-handed.

Filled with surprise, this friend surnamed Li went to find a friend surnamed Zhao who lived in the same alley, to tell him about tonight's "adventure."

"I know that woman, but I don't know her name. She used to 'pick up' old 'Lei' at the cinema. When old Lei left, she pestered old 'Li' at old Lei's apartment, asking him for money several times. Old Li avoided her in every possible way. Later, he ran into that woman on the street and blurted out that he had moved to 'No. 19, XX Lane'..."

"Oh no! No. 19, she's found me. I'm also an old Li!"

The next day, old Li met his beloved. "Darling! Thank you for the photograph. It has the magical power of 'Jiang Taigong is here, all gods retreat'..."

"What! Little rascal! Comparing me to Jiang Taigong? How unreasonable!"

When he told her about last night's "romantic encounter" nakedly, she couldn't stop laughing!

Referee Beaten Up Incident 260

— Zhi

The newspapers these two days introduce us to two good news; one is that the "Japanese Imperial Army" is again attacking Eastern Chahar, and the other is that a Jiangnan University Sports Association referee was beaten up by Jiaotong University students.

In this day and age, sports are particularly promoted, the king of balls is particularly prominent, and the appeal of ball games is more powerful than anything else. This is naturally due to the newspapers' advocacy, the educators' awards, which have created this vain trend. The beating of referees is precisely the result of this vain wind.

Once a year there is a Jiangnan University football match, and once a year there is a beating incident—either players are injured, or referees are beaten. Harming the lives of others is such a cruel act. Unfortunately, those future bachelors in the academy treat each other cruelly for a moment's vanity. The grand occasion of Jiangnan University's competition is just like that.

However, it is not right to completely blame the students for their barbarism. Those who run education take pride in promoting sports, and the school's equipment and students' studies are secondary. Winning a ball game is the most important thing, then, it is inevitable to buy players. The player's body is related to the school's honor, and he can be proud of himself and look down on everything. When it comes to the competition, he will naturally desperately try to win, otherwise, his value will be swept away, which is not worthwhile. Furthermore, the newspaper's publicity and the fans' devotion are also an enticement to the players to lift their chests and clench their fists.

Everything in China is developing in the wrong direction, and the whole society's heart is floating on the word vanity. The reason is that those who bear vanity can find a way to survive in this society. If a player wins a competition, he will be rewarded by the school, blown by the newspaper, and praised by the fans. That is a colorful, number one figure. Then, who wouldn't give his life for the battle, and who wouldn't take victory as the primary meaning! Naturally, those who are defeated will be frustrated, angry, vent, scold, and fight with fists and feet.

The occurrence of this kind of incident is naturally worthy of sighing for those who care, but I can briefly say that this is the end of the general public's pursuit of vanity, which is a phenomenon that is inevitably produced by the evolution of China's social environment. Educators should sigh when they see this incident, that China's education is bankrupt. But please ask the educators why they promoted the trophy competition, held swearing-in ceremonies, celebrations, etc., to motivate the enthusiasm of those players with the glory of "winning glory for learning"? The public opinionists also condemned this barbaric action when they saw this incident, but please ask the public opinionists why they are so enthusiastic about promoting vanity and publicizing the players' martial arts in such an extravagant way? Revolutionaries may be saddened by the nation's private struggles being too brave and public enemies being too cowardly when they see this incident, but, revolutionaries, what surrounds today's youth is all vanity, deception, and temptation. How can public anger arise?

Today's barbaric actions are full of the whole society. We cannot only blame the college students for being too barbaric. Today's education is all like this, and it cannot be said that education is bankrupt. Today, the psychology of the Chinese people is full of private fighting and anger, and we cannot blame these college students for being cowardly in the face of public enemies. If we want to blame, we can only blame today's Chinese society for being too bad, the society and the individual are separated day by day, the individual and the country are separated day by day, that is to say, the society, the country, and the individual have become three conflicting things that are manifested in today's Chinese real life.

In China, there is really nothing that is reasonable, that is holding the flag of justice. If we want to curse, we can only curse the entire society. Then, let us curse, curse those educators who buy players as "winning glory for the school"! Curse those public opinionists who encourage the general public to walk the path of vanity!

The referee who was injured should also be on the list of curses, curse him for being a puppet of vanity!

Broken Geese and Scattered Wild Geese 261

— Yiping

XX:

I bought a few books from the Commercial Press and came out, a car shining with electric light, illuminated by the sun, flew past me. Oh, XX, is that you? I almost shouted out. But the car had already headed north, a cloud of gasoline-smelling smoke still lingered in the air, two heads were printed on the rear window of the car, blurred, and finally nothing could be seen, only the smell of gasoline could be smelled.

XX, that gentleman sitting next to you is probably your husband. He has an awe-inspiring attitude, he has a car to ride in, in my few seconds of glimpse, his whole person is so lovely, your mother's pressure on you to marry him is fully justified, for your firm opposition at that time, almost letting go of a lifetime of good opportunity, I think you are too unwilling to plan for yourself.

Your mother only has you as a daughter, she is so clever in soliciting a good family with such suitable conditions for you, even if you don't plan for yourself, you have to understand the hard work of the old man. Do you know? The son-in-law has the reliance of half a son; if I were an old woman like your mother, the son-in-law in my mind might have more demanding conditions, otherwise I would rather my daughter be an old maiden, this is the lifelong event of a girl, not to mention that the mother still has the reliance of half a son!

The car has disappeared without a trace, and even the smell of gasoline has dissolved in the air. I am still staring at these few books and thinking about these things that have nothing to do with me. I am a man, and I will never have the psychology of a mother. Even if a man loves his daughter more than a mother does, I am an unmarried man, tens of millions of miles away from marriage, even if, to take ten thousand steps back (because my conditions are not suitable for every daughter's mother), a mother unexpectedly agrees to marry her daughter to me, but whether I can be a father to a daughter is something that no one can predict.

Returning to my small building, I stared blankly at the photo you gave me. I thought about it ecstatically. I regretted that I was not a daughter, I could hang up many conditions and solicit a companion for my lifelong event, like the gentleman next to you, he has an awe-inspiring attitude, he has a car to ride in, he is so lovely. Let my mother be happy and happy, he has a son-in-law with the reliance of half a son of that kind, after eating vegetarian food and chanting scriptures, wouldn't she smile wryly when she talks about it? Alas, I am a man!

The sky is gradually darkening, and things beyond a few feet cannot be seen in the small building. Your photos are also gradually blurring. I lean my head back and put my feet on the writing desk, learning the gentleman's demeanor and fantasizing, but unfortunately, there is a lack of a stylish cigar on the lips.

I am a man, and there is nothing I can do about it. However, I should have an awe-inspiring attitude, a car to ride in, so that people can see that I am so acceptable. I cannot make my own mother happy, but also make other people's mothers happy, and be a son-in-law with the conditions that are suitable for every mother's heart and with the reliance of half a son. However—I have nothing, only a man—a man who cannot make his own mother happy and other people's mothers happy!

So I felt sentimental. I, a man, was born into the world and have no benefit to anyone. I work every day, eat every day, for what? And it is so hard!

XX, you may think I am too "emotional," but I haven't heard the coquettish scolding of "emotional things" for a long time. Hey, probably, I am an "emotional man"!

Then I should work every day, eat every day, for the honorific title of the two words "emotion."

"Husband Who Pursues Stench"? 262

— Binfu

The weather is getting colder day by day, and people are all greedy for the warm bed. Who is happy to get up early in the morning to work? However, there are always people in the world who "do not enjoy happiness" and "do not know what is good for them." No matter how cold it is to "freeze the sky and the earth," every day when the dawn is just breaking, they loudly "ah—oh" to disturb the neighborhoods, which is exactly when people's sleep is the most intense! Not to mention the masters and mistresses, even Wang Ma and Zhang Ma are just about to close their eyes and rest. But they just have to "ah—oh" to disturb, which is undoubtedly what "the people in the quilts" hate, who are they? They are the workers who dump the chamber pots.

The workers who dump the chamber pots are men and women, old and young. Probably every manure cart is always paired with a man and a woman, one pushing and one pulling, and the relationship between this man and woman, father and daughter, mother and son, of course, exists, but the most common is husband and wife.

If the working hours of news reporters are at night, and the working hours of bank and foreign firm staff are during the day, then the working hours of the workers who dump the chamber pots are in the early morning after the night and before the day.

They crawl out of the quilts every day before it dawns, pushing or pulling the "chamber pot" cart to the street. The wife is barefoot, and the husband is also barefoot. The wife's chest is tied with the rope of the "manure cart," she puts her feet on the ground with force, and her body is prostrate parallel to the ground, using all her strength to drag; the husband's body is also bent parallel to his wife, pushing forward with force; sometimes maybe the husband is pulling and the wife is pushing. They go east and west like this, the husband shouts "ah," the wife answers "oh," to knock on the back doors of everyone's houses, to load the excrement of every household's men, women, old and young.

Don't the workers who dump the chamber pots have a look at love? Don't they have the same mood as the mistresses and masters to sleep a little longer in the warm quilt? What limits this mood is their duty, what forces them to

Page 17

them to this job is their life.

The disgust for excrement is the genius of human beings. Thus, it indirectly makes people not have a good impression of the workers who dump the chamber pots. If they unfortunately encounter a manure cart on the road, there is simply no one who does not reveal a look of "being horrified" and "going away in a sullen manner."

Are the men and women who dump the chamber pots all born "husbands who pursue stench"? Those who listen clearly should know that this is "not entirely true."

Their feelings are the same as the people all over the world, but under the whip of life, they have to do this against their nature.

"Excretion" is the natural result of animals. If they don't do this work, the consequences are really unimaginable—their work is difficult and hard, but their rewards are meager, how great they are—are they "husbands who pursue stench"? "Living in leisure without teaching" and only knowing how to speculate and profit are the real "husbands who pursue stench!"

Every time I see a couple pulling a chamber pot cart, I often admire and envy their spirit of cooperation, and I feel that a perfect family should be built on this spirit.

Hungry for Whole Days and Nights of Rain 263

— Liehuo

Fortunately, during the January 28th Shanghai War, I didn't go hungry, but after the everlasting Shanghai Truce Agreement, I returned to my hometown and was hungry for two whole days and nights on the Xiang-E railway line. This is a page in my life that I will never forget.

On the night when the Eastern Ocean soldiers began to bombard Tiantong'an, I once again had a conflict and broke with Mr. Fang because of the harsh treatment. Mr. Fang also knew that it was impossible to recover—my wife and old master all advised me, but I still rolled up my quilt and wanted to leave, but unexpectedly, Mr. Fang's good friend Mr. Xi knocked on the door urgently downstairs.

Mr. Xi, like a snail, hurriedly turned up to the small building, and said in a mess without a head: "Mr. X, it's started, oh, it's terrible! Is Mr. Fang asleep? Is Mr. Fang asleep?" Before I could answer, Mr. Fang, whose sense of smell and hearing was as sensitive as a cat and dog, actually knew without error that his good friend Mr. Xi had come. Half of his oily head appeared at the door of the front厢房, and simply said these five words: "Mr. Xi, please come in!"

Mr. Xi went upstairs, and I re-evaluated my vague future. The Eastern Ocean soldiers are fighting, this, from the perspective of the entire nation-state, will undoubtedly overturn the ancestral graves of thousands of generations: but for me, it is always a good opportunity to escape this cage. The news is indeed very tight, and from now on, maybe there is no way to survive; however, I am confident that I can be a volunteer army. Old Qian has already gone, he will definitely introduce me, give up my life, and fight against Japanese imperialism, fight against all imperialism, I will definitely leave this prison, I have been wronged enough in the past year.

Just as I was evaluating this, Mr. Xi came in; "Mr. Fang sincerely asked me to come and keep you, the news is so tight, Mr. X, please stay, stay!" As he spoke, he unpacked my quilt, which was of course pointed out to him by Mr. Fang. In front of the unfamiliar Mr. Xi, I was a little embarrassed to turn my face, so I couldn't help but "um" vaguely. It turned out that Mr. Fang was standing outside the door, stretched his foot and stepped into the small building, smiling and saying: "Please forgive everything! Thank you for helping, helping!"

In this way, during the terrifying Shanghai War, fortunately, I didn't go hungry again. The truce was agreed, and traffic had returned to normal, so I carried out another form of prison escape, that is; asked for a month's leave to return to my hometown to visit relatives. Mr. Fang actually agreed, only saying that I must not exceed one month's leave.

On my long return journey, it was safe from Shanghai to Hankou. The terror was on the Xiang-E road. In order to hurry, I and Yun商定 agreed that we would take the train back; because taking a steamboat would take at least a day and two nights, while the train would not take a day. I still remember that the departure was at 7 pm in the evening, and it was scheduled to arrive in Changsha tomorrow morning, but unexpectedly, after driving out for two sections of small stations fifteen miles away, it turned back again. It is said that the coal and water were not enough, but some people said that there was trouble ahead. Later, the car still went out wanting to go in and retreat. When it arrived at Puzhi, it stopped moving forward, and suddenly there was chaos in the first and second class carriages, saying that the bandits were full of both sides of the railway, and a large number of wounded soldiers just rushed into our fourth class carriage. This is the suffering we must endure. Although the first and second class carriages are empty, the wounded soldiers are going to rush into our fourth class carriage, which is already crowded with people.

Let the blood and tears of the wounded soldiers flow, let the hoarse throats scream, they are ending the meaning of life in their dreams!

It stopped for two whole days. The usual hawkers who were too many did not know where they had gone. I got off the bus to urinate and found a corpse selling pancakes on the side of the road.

After being hungry for two full days and nights, we finally arrived in Changsha in terror. I didn't go hungry during the Shanghai War, but I suffered this scene after the truce agreement. Heaven or man?

Novel

Shanghai (27) 264

— Zhang Laosan

(40) Now is not the time for our love

The letter read:

Brother,

To be honest, being in Shanghai for nearly a year has given me too much grief. My departure is also out of helplessness. Brother, I will always remember that now is not the time for love, especially since I am a woman who cannot marry.

Being oppressed by my uncle in the countryside was not something I could easily endure. I resolutely sacrificed my reputation and threw myself into the arms of Shanghai. But what has Shanghai given me? Although I myself have not fully implemented my set intentions, I also take a share of the blame. Brother, I am not a love-supremacy advocate who says that love is life. I also do not want to snatch you over as my prisoner; but I love you is a fact that cannot be hidden from you. On the train, in the hotel, and finally when we stepped into the Zhengyi Society together, you did not reject my love, which is also a fact that you cannot hide from me. As for Huixing appearing in front of us, I thought it was not worth competing with others, but I did not expect that a man's heart is so easy to change. Brother, I will always, always remember that now is not the time for our love, from your first sentence to your last sentence, so I left.

Women are inherently jealous. I think my departure may be judged with such an unwarranted accusation. I myself do not admit to being a woman, because I am too ignorant of the female nature of jealousy, I failed. Although I can do my best to snatch you over, I am confident that I have this confidence, but I am unwilling to do this kind of behavior that forces people to do what they don't want to do, because I am not a woman and do not have the inherent jealousy of women. And—brother, now is not the time for our love?

I am leaving, I will dedicate myself to work that is more important than love. The iron hooves of imperialism are eyeing people for devouring. I hope that the comrades of Zhengyi will work hard to achieve your set goals, or we may meet again in a certain place. Remember, I will say loudly to the comrades of Zhengyi Society: "Now is not the time for our love!"

Goodbye, brother, goodbye, comrades of Zhengyi Society.

"Good! I will never dream of being a woman again, now is not the time for our love!" Xiao Huang threw down the letter and stood up, posing with a serious face as if making a vow. "Our loyal comrade!" I patted his shoulder, and the matter about Sister Min had calmed down.

"Comrade!" He joined his heels and raised his hand, a military salute that could not be more natural to him.

"Now is not the time for our love!" I tore the letter to pieces and waved it in the air, and the paper scraps danced like butterflies.

Film Special

Where is Charles Farrell Now? 265

— Guang Dao

He has returned to the screen to film new movies.

And a very valuable conversation.

A few days ago at the Grand Shanghai, I watched "Paddy the Next Best Thing" starring Janet Gaynor, alongside Warner Baxter. After watching, many people remembered Janet Gaynor's old partner of eight or nine years, Charles Farrell, and happily asked, where has Charles Farrell gone, since we haven't seen him for so long? Therefore, I think this news is what everyone is eager to know, so I will report his recent news and conversations.

According to recent news, Charles Farrell, after a long rest, has now returned to Hollywood and is starting to film again. His first film after returning to the screen is called "Aggie Appleby", produced by RKO. It is said that since leaving Fox, he has been unwilling to sign long-term contracts with any company. He is only willing to work if he has a good script. Otherwise, he would rather sacrifice financial income than shoot films casually. This is because he doesn't want to disappoint the audience. He once left Warner Brothers, and recently left Fox, because the company did not have satisfactory roles for him, forcing him to leave. Now that he has returned to the screen, he seems determined to uphold his principles, not to make bad films, and not to be bound by long-term contracts. Here are some recent remarks:

"I used to be too kind and too casual. That's why they all called me 'Easy-going Charlie'. But in Hollywood, that's a disadvantage. If you don't take yourself seriously, people won't value you either. To succeed in Hollywood, you must be like on a battlefield, establishing a front line." These are Farrell's thoughts. He has recognized his past mistakes. This time he returns to the screen with a fighting spirit. He also said: "I used to be too kind, without a defensive line to the outside world. This virtue of peace developed too much, leading to many drawbacks. I was willing to take on any role that others didn't want to do. So many other actors rushed ahead to compete for good films, and even bargained with the company, while I waited behind for people to choose. I took what was left without complaint. Over time, the company understood that Charles Farrell was an easy-going gentleman who was easy to please, and gradually they paid less attention to him."

This is the case with most things in the world. As for the virtue of peace and the spirit of humility, they are certainly good; but "too much is as bad as too little". Being too humble often invites humiliation. In the case of a country, the doctrine of non-resistance can lead to the loss of the country, which has already been proven. In the case of an individual, if a person is in society and only retreats and yields, without a spirit of progress, it is not a good thing either. So being too competitive is not good, and being too yielding is not good. Charles Farrell's words really contain many philosophies of social life. He also said:

"If I were a little stronger, regarded myself as a big star, and had a firm position when dealing with outsiders, not just talking about friendship, then the company would not dare, nor would they be willing, to give me the roles that others didn't want. I have seen many actors who are not as good as me achieve victory in disputes with the company. What's the reason? It is because the boundaries between public and private matters are clearly defined. Business is business, and emotions are not allowed to interfere." These words are not necessarily just for Charles Farrell, or a movie actor, but for anyone. As the saying goes, "Respect his appearance, and people will also respect him." Otherwise, if you look down on yourself, people will also look down on you.

Film Review

Review of "The Misleading Lady" 266

— Moore

"The Misleading Lady"

Movie authorities often like to use the word "banned" for publicity. This method of seizing the audience's psychology is naturally very effective, but in Shanghai, because there is a distinction between the concession and non-concession areas, there are often many films that cannot be shown in the concession areas, so they are shown in the non-concession theaters. Thus, "The Misleading Lady," which was banned by the concession authorities, was shown at the Shanghai Grand Theater, which had screened the famous Soviet films "Life" and "Jinshan".

In fact, in "The Misleading Lady", we cannot find any reason for it to be banned. It is just an ordinary romantic comedy. People at the end of the century, because they are aware that they have no future, and while they have not yet fallen, they try to entertain themselves as much as possible. The reflection of this mentality of "If I don't enjoy myself now, the days will pass" is the main reason for the production of general wine and women films. Naturally, because of various factual restrictions, even if they want to enjoy themselves as much as possible, it is still impossible. So they can only imagine all kinds of unexpected adventures. As for whether it is reasonable or not, they don't care, and only the unreasonable fits their fantasies. Needless to say, "The Misleading Lady" is like this. It is inevitable that they turn this kind of story into a comedy, because their creation of this story will not be written into a tragedy to make themselves miserable. As the saying goes, "Meet wine and laugh, how much can life be"!

Of course, in "The Misleading Lady", their boredom with life is vented, but this is not intentional.

Truly excellent old artists clearly understand their own destiny and cannot hide their sorrow. Others who are a little more ambiguous are not like this. The reason why there are more comedies and fewer tragedies in European and American films now is this relationship.

Claudette Colbert's success in "Cleopatra" was due to the guidance of a great director, but in "The Misleading Lady" it is much less successful. She is neither lively, nor does she have any facial expressions, but the play requires facial expressions everywhere.

Christmas in Hollywood 267

— Dong Lin

Christmas in Hollywood always feels too warm, like wearing a fur coat and sipping ice cream, but the reality is not entirely like that. Although the outside is bathed in warm sunshine, it is snowing in the house! Snowmen made of white cotton also appear with cars full of drunks.

When the chapel on Beverly Hills rings the Christmas bells, what strikes the stars are: gift boxes piled up like mountains from fans, and the sound of telephones ringing between parties, constantly ringing...

In addition, this year there is also a surprising box for evening banquets. This box is made of colored paper, with slender paper tubes hanging on both sides. If you pull the two ends of the paper tube hard, there will be a "pop" and a military hat with "Hero Napoleon" written on it will fly out, followed by a doll's head wearing the military hat, with a cigar in its mouth. Then, with another "pop", a card with "This year's La, Falentine" written on it pops out. The guests around laugh like "idiot's laughter", ha ha ha...

Extra Edition of "Flame of Youth" 268

— Santa Claus

Performed at the Carlton at the end of the year

And send autographed photos of the stars

The colleagues of Tianyi Company elected "Flame of Youth" as the champion work of 1933, which is indeed the company's effort. The film was sent to Beijing for review after it was completed last month. It has now been reviewed and has been shipped from Beijing to Shanghai. It is now scheduled to be premiered at the Carlton Grand Theater on the 29th of this month. The performance of the star Chen Yu-mei in the film has a special breakthrough. Ms. Chen considers it to be her proud work. Director Qiu Qixiang also made many amazing contributions. The suggestive hints are also very wonderful. In addition, the newly discovered Oriental model beauty Ye Qiuxin co-starred, which added a lot of color to the film. The photography skills and lighting are better than the previous works of Tianyi. For the sake of thanking the audience who love to watch her works, the star Chen Yu-mei specially printed 3,000 exquisite New Year cards and distributed them to all circles in this city. All those who receive Chen Yu-mei's New Year card and bring the card to the Carlton to "watch the Flame of Youth" can exchange for a recent small photo of Ms. Chen Yu-mei, signed by her, to commemorate the audience of "Flame of Youth".

Here, let us turn to the Christmas postcards of the stars. Below is a description of the postcard patterns of several stars:

Jack Oakie's: A maid is kissing the ice store clerk, the ice melts, the cat jumps, and the bouquet jumps into the air.

Norma Shearer's: In a silver world, two red little deer are dancing, doesn't this completely express her mood?

Jackie Cooper's: Santa Claus is riding a small boat, crossing waves as high as mountains, heading towards "The World of Children".

Janet Gaynor's: A girl making a snowman, a bright moon hanging over the woods, with the words "This is a very cold snowman, but I wish you a happy Christmas with great enthusiasm"!

Fang Peilin is "Xiao Wan" 269

— Bi Bi

Set designer Fang Peilin is probably from Ningbo, so many people call him Brother Afang.

It is said that Brother Afang is twenty-seven years old this year, but he is still unmarried. At a banquet, Afang's fellow villager Ying Yunwei proposed that everyone should call Fang Peilin "Xiao Wan" (Ningbo dialect for "child").

Many people asked him why? He replied:

"The rules in Ningbo are that anyone who has not married a wife, whether he is sixty or seventy years old, is called 'Xiao Wan'." At that time, everyone at the banquet laughed.

However, Brother Afang is going to marry a wife next spring. Then, the time to be "Xiao Wan" is at most only a few dozen days.

Yuan Meiyun Practices Large Calligraphy 270

Tan Ying said: "Female stars should know a few words, otherwise, it is very inconvenient to go anywhere." Therefore, there are several female stars now, such as Wang Renmei, Li Lili, and Tan Ying, who are still in school.

Yuan Meiyun, the star of "The Angry Tide of the Chinese Sea", is very intelligent. Although she did not spend much time in school, her knowledge is already considerable. Usually, when she has free time, her father often teaches her to read, so her literature has improved day by day. Recently, Yuan Meiyun gets up every morning and practices a page of large calligraphy without interruption. I have seen her large characters, and they have indeed made great progress.

This is truly a rare female star, I think. (Que Chou)

"Sports Queen" Golden Palace Feast Busy 271

Since the Lianhua Second Factory started filming "Sports Queen", it has received a lot of help from the education and sports circles, so it has been holding grand feasts in the Golden Palace for days, with the Sports Queen personally bestowing imperial wine to express her condolences. A few days ago, it also hosted a banquet for the Shanghai Provincial Middle School and the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education Normal School. The two schools strongly supported Lianhua's production of this film, which promotes the popularity of sports and promotes the true spirit of sports. When filming the location of the sports meeting, Shanghai Middle School selected 100 male and female scouts, 20 military band members, 20 medical team members, and two scout tents to maintain order and participate in the performance. Liangjiang also selected 40 female athletes to support the event. Lianhua Company expressed its heartfelt gratitude for the brave and generous support of the two schools and other news, education, and sports circles, because in European and American countries, film companies can often get the full support of all circles, which is rare in China.

Film Novel

Shanghai 24 Hours (6) 272

— Tian Fu

Wow! Good fellow! He stole something and actually used the money to do good deeds generously. This is a "criminal" act! It is a pity that this act was not seen by the comprador or the comprador's wife, otherwise, would he still be able to "get away with it" like this?

But naturally, the comprador and his wife will not see Lao Zhao. They will never be together. At this time, the wife is sleeping sweetly in the mansion. And the comprador is busy working in the yarn factory at this time. - Half an hour ago, the comprador was summoned to the office of the yarn factory's manager. The manager has a small goatee under his nose and is short. He is a person with an "exotic flavor". His attitude is solemn and awe-inspiring, seemingly more impressive than the comprador. And the comprador seems very humble and respectful in front of him.

The manager said: "The northern area has recently returned to the state before the war, but the business in Shanghai and the Yangtze River basin is not good: this is your responsibility!"

The comprador did not get angry when he heard this lesson. "Yes, yes," he kept saying "yes" in his mouth, thinking about a clever plan to expand the business for the manager. - Now this clever plan has been approved by the manager and he has returned to the factory to implement it.

At this time, the comprador is busy: directing the factory staff to tear off the original labels on all the yarn bales and replace them with new labels - the labels are prominently printed with the words: "Completely Domestic Goods". Due to the comprador's loyalty, these many foreign yarn bales marked "Completely Domestic Goods" will soon flow into the domestic goods market in an endless stream, and then be delivered to the hands of the buyers (who are of course Chinese). But who knows the secret of the "clever plan" in this?

(9) The Punished Soul

Time crawls forward second by second. The life of the injured child laborer is becoming shorter. His body lies stiffly, motionless; but his chest rises and falls violently: his throat is like bellows, breathing difficultly and urgently. His eyes are half open and half closed, and the eyeballs have gone somewhere, leaving only a line of gray sclera.

The sister-in-law of the sick child whose business was suspended by the comprador's mansion sits beside him, watching this scene, and her heart feels like something is stabbing hard needle by needle. Lao Zhao's doctor has been invited, but the doctor only looked at the lying child, said nothing, shook his head disappointedly and left. The child's expression looks more and more wrong, as if smiling but not smiling, with his eyes half open like that. Chen Da's woman is getting anxious and just shouts for help, calling "Brother, brother!"

She shouts, but it is useless even if she shouts herself hoarse: the brother rolls his eyes and dies.

The sister-in-law cries and cannot lift her head. Standing next to her without saying a word, shedding tears, is Lao Zhao, who just invited the doctor. (To be continued)
